命令 1

國民政府十二日令任命李益滋·應振復·馬吉第爲軍事參謀院參議、此令、又令、李明·霍揆彰·李默庵·吳良琛給予四等寳鼎章、此令、又令、兼行政院院長蔣中正呈、據軍政部部長何應欽呈、秘書徐恭典總務廳科員陳彬如·張揆肅·軍需署軍械司科員蔡馥生·兵工署技術員王濟安等、另候任用、陸軍署軍械司科員黎盛茀、兵工署秘書楊柳風、技術員陳運晟等、呈懇辭職、總務廳科員沈玢·航空署科員馬驤·軍需署營造司、技正鄔振賡·科員吳開邀·副官宣堦·兵工署科員李國典等、另有任用、均請免職、應照准、此令、又令兼行政院院長蔣中正呈、據軍政部部長何應欽呈、請任命黃勛爲軍政部總務廳科員、沈玢爲軍政部陸軍署總務署科員、孫學斌爲軍政部陸軍署軍械司科員、夏詒藀爲軍政部軍需署營造司技正、宣堦爲軍政部軍需署營造局科員、端木宕爲軍政部軍需署營造司副官、虞怡祖爲軍政部兵工署秘書、朱文伯爲軍政部兵工署科員、周修齋·吳增耆·金毓麟·胡宗璞爲軍政部兵工署技術員、應照准此令、

五中全會今日准可開會 2

在京中委已有二十一人

（南京）五中全會已定十三晨八時、在中央黨部舉行開會式、其秩序已由中央秘書處擬就、茲探錄如下、㈠中央委員就位、㈡奏樂、㈢唱黨歌、㈣向黨國旗及總理遺像、行三鞠躬禮、㈤主席恭讀總理遣囑、㈥靜默三分鐘、㈦主席致開會詞、㈧奏樂、㈨攝影、㈩禮成、又黨部佈置、亦由

庶務科辦理完竣、於大門二門各搭彩樓一座、大門橫額爲「統一意志圑結精神」、對聯爲「遵行訓政時期約法、力謀民國長治久安、」二門橫額爲「中國國民黨第三屆中央執行委員第五次全體會議開會式」、對聯爲「鞏固統一、確保和平」、禮堂橫額、爲「親愛精神」、對聯爲「實行國民會議决議、努力訓政建設工作」、其餘各處、亦均懸掛彩花、氣象煥然一新、（十二日專電）、

（南京）五中全會最大目的、爲接受國民會議决議案、决定四全代會日期、及依據約法、修改國府組織法、同時仍法重行任命各院部會長、並對蔣所持專力剿匪之態度、將有慰勉表示、至各中委提案、聞並不多、因國民會議議决案、已爲全國民意之結晶、祗須努力施行、便可利民福國、即有少數提案、亦無非關於推進黨務事等宜、（十二日專電）

（南京）五中全會法定人數十九人、現在京已有二十一人、明日開會無問題、蔣擬十六日離京、一說十八日赴廬山、（十二日專電）

飛機墜落中山路上

駕駛員幸未受重傷

（南京）中央軍校航空班學員王某、十二日下午四時、自駕練習機、由明故宮飛機塲起飛練習，因内部機件，發生阻碍，致發動機突然停止、機身即於距地面約四十分尺之高度、墜落於中山路中央醫院門首、機翼下覆、發動機及機翼均有損壞、該駕駛員雖略受震盪、幸未受重傷、當將該機運往修理塲修理、（十二日專電）

輔助敎育事業的：世界商業儲蓄銀行 12

發起：：熱心敎育事業深有銀行經騐的份子所組織

目的：：提取股東應得紅利之一部份補助貧民敎育

註册：：國民政府財政部給照立案實業部註册照准

已於六月三日開始營業

六月底前加利息有贈品

年來上海金融界之盛况，爲向來所未有，獨於致力敎育事業之銀行，尙付缺如，近始有熱心敎育事業而深有銀行經騐之世界書局一部份有志股東，組織世界商業儲蓄銀行於上海，最高企望，欲以銀行毎年盈餘之一部份，卽章程上所規定股東應得紅利百分之五十中，提出五十分之十分以補助貧民敎育，財政部銀字第六十一號執照，早以頒給，實業部亦已註册有案，總行在上海四馬路世界里，自本月三日正式開業以業，歷時未久，聲譽已播動國内外，其營業分商業，儲蓄二部，商業爲（一）商業定期存欵，期限自三個月至十年（二）商業活期存欵（三）商業往來存欵（四）往來透支存欵，均可隨時支取，儲蓄爲（一）活期儲蓄存欵（二）整存整取儲蓄，期限自一年至十五年（三）普通零存整取，期限自一年至十五年（四）特種零存整取，期限自一月至十五年（五）整存零取儲蓄，期限自一年至十五年（六）按期支息儲蓄，期限自一年至十年（七）對本對利儲蓄，期限一律七足年，所定利率，較其他爲高，例如活期儲蓄存欵，有週息七厘，毎六個月結算一次，利上生利，又如整存整取儲蓄，週息自九厘五毫至一分二厘，自爲其他儲蓄機關所不及，更能鑒於一般社會生活維艱，分訂各項儲蓄方法，以文字促一般人從速覺悟，利用儲蓄，爲自身將來保障，例如另存整取儲蓄類乙項，假定將來欲得養老費一萬元者，如定期十五年，則毎月祗須繳存洋十九元三角，期滿卽可提取洋一萬元，定期十年者，毎月存洋四十四元六角，期滿亦得洋一萬元，又如整存整取儲蓄類甲項，如一次存入洋一千八百廿六元九角六分，定期十五年，亦得洋一萬元，整存整取儲蓄類乙類，今日存入洋一百元，定期十五年，可得洋五百六十二元三角五分，如今日存入洋五千元，定期十年，可得洋一萬四千六百九十七元一角五分、十五年則可得洋二萬八千一百十七元七角之鉅、或則積少成多、輕而易舉，或則祗存一次，手續簡捷，無往不宜，洵是有益人羣之最大貢獻，一切細則，訂有專章，隨時可向索取，更聞在六月底以前，爲開業紀念期，期内向存各項儲蓄，或照章再增加利息一厘，或加贈世界書局之書券，或各種精美贈品，紀念箋册等等，以引起儲蓄人之興趣，苦以孤詣爲社會服務，無微不至如此，得大多數人之欽崇讚美，固亦宜矣，Ａ１２３４

時評

日内田繼任滿鐵總裁 13

今日東京電。日滿鐵總裁仙石辭職。閣議以是缺對華關係重要。决以曾任外相代首相及駐華公使之大人物内田康哉氏繼任。此亦爲我國人極應注意之一事也。

滿鐵爲中日交涉最重要之懸案。而今日中日兩國委員。正將東北開議。日人方面以此會議。爲日本在華權利攸關。而又鑒於中國廢除不平等條約之倡導。懾於外間鐵路綱之宣傳。大有疑心生暗鬼急起抵抗之象。觀其近日所發表之對外同志會宣言。對鐵道問題。决主强硬化。對其他權益。决以緊急處置。日本朝野名士。列名發起者甚多。公爵男爵。亦有多人在内。可見日人之處心積慮。欲堅决擁護其所謂滿鐵旣得權者。已無可諱。今者内田氏之繼任總裁。據謂係若槻首相尊重西園寺公之意見而推舉之。質言之即尊重一般元老之鐵路政策也。内田氏雖號稱超然派。然旣爲老派人物。其思想政策。必不輕易變更。且其任駐華公使時代。去今雖遠。當時日本之對華外交政策。國人尙能記憶。今以時代過去之外交家。當今日南滿鐵路之重任。倘若迎合日人一時之狂獗之潮流。忘其爲平等世界。堅持向來一貫之政策而猛力進行。則今後東北之鐵路交涉。更難樂觀矣。

王伯羣談時局 19

廣東局面决難持久

剿匪工作積極進行

（南京）本報記者頃訪王伯羣、關於時局情形、有所詢問、承彼一一見答、爰分述如次、

（問）部長抱恙甚久、已否回復健康、（答）初係足疾復發、繼染傷寒、照西醫慣例、須靜養四星期、故回京期不免稽延、當余病時、恰値多事之秋、各方頗多猜疑、現旣回部服務、謡言自息、

（問）部長對廣東事件、有何感想、（答）余忍廣東事件、爲去年北平擴會的廻光返照、擴會失敗後、反動派常欲伺隙而動、如胡先生去職事發生、彼等認爲絶好機會、聳動陳濟棠、在粤發難、然苦於勢孤、不得不聯絡張桂軍、更連帶及於組派、與張桂軍的同盟者、回想汪精衛與胡先生過去的歷史、及胡先生去歲反對擴會的决心、乃少數反動分子、竟欲將其牽入游渦、破壞胡先生名譽、寗非夢想、

（問）依部長觀察、廣東事件、將來如何演變、（答）現在廣東的重要脚色、其信仰意見歷史、各各不同、情感上更是敵友混雜、斷無成事之理、據最近消息、張惠長陳策、已表示消極、汪精衛與陳濟棠、因改組省黨部、發生極大意見、孫哲生退還省主席委狀後、雖以林雲陔承乏、然因事事牽制、已經灰心、故廣東局面、决難持久、

（問）中央對粤事、究取若何態度、（答）據余所知、中央始終抱和平統一態度、但如果彼等終不覺悟、甘爲禍首、故亦有相當準備、

（問）江西剿匪情形如何、（答）迭接何敬之部長來電、赤匪自聞粤事發生、負嵎頑抗冀圖蔓延、惟中央認定、剿匪爲中國民族存亡問題、較粤事尤爲重要、故對剿匪工作、仍積極猛進、

（問）盛傳交鐵兩部、有合併消息、確否、（答）此項問題、權在中央、余因地位關係、未便發表意見、

（問）部長最近登報啓事、與保女士結婚、其經過可得聞乎、（答）余於十七年冬、元配逝世、家慈以余内助需人、屢令續絃、親友和之、物色介紹、日不暇給、余因舊式婚姻、毎多不滿、遂謝親友、而自行留意、保君季新、本係好友、常相往還、因得識其猶女志寗、志寗勤學、無時下風、於去冬大學畢業後、家慈因年老多疾、促余續絃益急、於是始託親友作伐、得其家長同意、婚約始定、外間謡言、謂係重金納妾、自有事實上證明、不足置辯、（十二日專電）

接要聞 79

收捐税、其故因中俄會議近商條約尙未决定、一經收税（則俄方即可藉口中國承認其復交通商、即可大批運貨來華、）現毎週間裝貨若干車、分運各大小站、即於火車上售銷、有人詢之、則自稱爲活動消費社、但東鐵消費社宗旨、除日用品外、均不准售賣、并不准賣與非鐵路職員、今則一概不問、且恐非路員不買、毎於貨到各站時、派員四處宣傳、招徠中外人士、登車購買、其貨物因旣未納税、且不負東鐵運費、售價低廉、銷行大暢、毎一星期、至少毎一小站、可售賣一火車、大站二三火車不等、緣是各地商店、大受影響、哈埠消費總社、亦特别活動、故凡大百貨店如同發隆·公和利·阜和昶·恒順昌、均受影響、各商爲防前途危害計、日前紛向總商會、請求轉呈官廳禁止俄商假名活動、此外特區商聯會亦於日前召開大會、議决呈請官方反業東鐵消費社復活、當局對於此事、已函致外交特派員鍾毓、向駐哈俄領交涉矣、並聞蘇俄政府、規定凡東鐵服務之赤系路員、毎月以其所得薪金四之一爲生活費、四之一爲黨費、其餘四之二、用爲擴張活動消費社底欵、毎月可得百七十餘萬、故其力量頗爲雄厚也、（七日）

淸華學生組武力護校圑 100

誓死拒絶吳南軒返校

｜敎授學生代表赴京｜

北平十二日電淸華全體學生今晨大會、議决、誓死拒絶吳南軒返校、組織武力護校圑、並電敎部、謂原有敎授以未接得下屆聘書將全體離校他就、請設法續聘、

全國運動大會籌備委員會、鑒於現屆開會期邇、

各種運動比賽規則、亟應積極編訂付印、至此種規則、泰半均採用世界及遠東運動會所訂定者、惟其中亦有重要變更多點、茲爲使各地明晰及供預備者之參加起見、特擇錄如下、

男子跳欄 126

男子四百米跳欄、毎一路線應設欄十架、欄高九一·四五的米突、自起跑線至第一架欄之距離爲四十五米、各欄間之距離爲三十五米、自第十架至終點綫之距離爲四十米、

女田徑賽 127

（甲）八十米跳欄、毎一路綫應設欄八架、欄高七六·二生的米突、（二呎半）自起跑綫至第一架欄及自第八架欄至終點綫之距離、均爲十三米、各欄間之距離爲八米、（乙）標槍、（一）（構造）木製裝以鐵或銅質之尖頭、槍之重以點與槍尖之距離、不得過九五生的米突·或短於八○生的米突、（二）（把手處）在重心點處繞以闊十六生的米突之弦綫爲把手處、弦綫須光匀無結節、其兩端之圓徑、不得較槍桿大過二五密里米突、槍桿上除把手之弦綫外、不得有其他相類物件、（三）（長短）全體至少長二二○生的米突、（四）（重量）不得輕於六○○格萊姆、

男子籃球 128

凡在中圈跳球、球未逹到最高點時、不得拍球球未拍出前、不得離開中圈、拍球至多兩次、未經其他八人中之任何一人接觸或觸及地面、或球籃或遮板、中鋒不得再行觸球、又球員正擲在籃時、對手有犯侵人規則者、如該球因此未能擲中、應罰兩球、如該球依然擲中而有效者、則僅罰球、至女子籃球仍用雙區制、

男子排球 129

（發球）球員毎次發球、准有一次失誤、如連續失誤二次、即爲失敗、而其對隊乃得一分、

男女網球 130

採用台維斯杯賽法、毎隊至多四人、毎兩隊互相之比賽、共有單打四次、雙打一次、先爲甲隊第一單打對乙隊第一單打、甲隊第二單打對乙隊第二單打、次作雙打、然後甲隊第一單打對乙對第二單打、乙隊第一單打對甲隊第二單打前後單打、均須原人、惟雙方可以散換其餘二球員、

最後一單勝華僑

（大阪通訉）菲利賓桑托瑪大學籃球隊自渡日遠征以來、無攻不克、無戰不勝、橫掃日本全國、技藝之超羣、致人人稱嘆、在日計戰十三塲、均獲全勝、獲球總數計在千分以上、毎次表演、無不驚人、在東京計九戰九勝、對各大學比賽之成績、業誌二日本報、其在關西四戰、已均告捷、而比數亦頗令人捧腹、對大阪學生隊之一幕、竟産生百餘分之怪紀錄、可謂空前之奇事、而最後一戰、係對神户華僑、斯幕最爲精彩、因華僑反抗毫不示弱、桑大在大阪神户兩處獲勝之成績誌下、

黨部消息 141

㈠市執委會之注意、本市黨部以提倡國貨、爲黨部七項運動之一、且國貨爲杜塞毎年十二萬萬漏巵之利器、今帝國主義者、深恐經濟侵略、大受打擊、以先發制人之手段、縱令捕房封閉、認爲藐視華商、侵害國權、因於昨日第一百十五次常會提出討論、經議决、函請市政府向公共租界當局嚴重交涉矣、㈠三區黨部之宣言、三區黨部昨日發表宣言云、（上略竊本市中華國産商場、爲推銷國貨之樞紐、近則遭忌於英捕房、假藉名義、用非法手段、擅行封閉、毆擊職員、橫蠻不堪、聆悉之下、殊深憤慨查帝國主義者、恃科學之發逹、機械之進步、以剩餘商品、爲對華經濟侵略之唯一方策、國産商場之設立、實與其此種侵略主義、根本相衝突、英帝國主義者統治下之捕房、遂不惜假藉該塲游藝部份執照問題、非法予以封閉、夫該處之爲新世界游藝塲、已歷有年所、而國産商場之遷入、則未及兼旬、如以謂設備未週或房屋欠固、而予以封閉、則何以給照於開設新世界游藝塲之時、而獨予封閉於國産商塲開業之日、且該商塲舖設於樓下、而游藝部份、則在樓上、如認其以游藝部份未給執照、故予封閉爲理由、則僅須停止或封閉其游藝部份已足、而何以必須連及於商塲部份、反復推考、謂非别具用意、實不可得、而毆辱職員、擅行拘捕、尤足顯露其帝國主義者之猙獰面目、惟以吾國家領土之内、而一任其橫蠻若此、試靜心瞑目思之、尙復成何體統、而此事之發生、適當本市公共租界華顧問華會辦就職後之七日、實予吾人以極大之敎訓、使知求枝枝節節之解决之不可恃、冀與帝國主義者講斤論價政策之不足取、應本總理大無畏之精神、遵照國民會議所指示、一致努力於廢約運動、使得整個之解决、而爲一勞永逸之圖、本會除謹率全區黨員、擴大宣傳外、謹此宣言、諸維亮察、

英艦被撞後仍無確訊 168

海昌公司再電詢問

是否毓大尙難證實

本埠海昌輪船局毓大輪、與英國潛永艦柏斯登號相撞後、海昌公司昨再電詢眞相、各國政府、亦均電弔溺斃士兵、茲將昨日所得情形、分誌如下、

再電詢問　毓大輪上海代理之海昌輪船公司、自得招商局圖南輪無線電後、得悉毓大輪與英潛水艦相撞、曾電往詢問、前日得來電、並未說明肇事情形、因此懷疑莫决、十一日下午十時、電營口詢問眞相云、「通開貨三百悉、報載大途撞沉英潛艦、確否、覆、」及至昨晨仍未得復電、於上午十二時又電云、「各報紛載大在途撞沉英潛艦、確否、急復、」直至下午九時、仍未得復電、

各國電弔　英潛水艦柏斯登號、在山東西北角四十英里與毓大輪相撞下沉後、溺斃兵士十八人、美潛艦皮岡號、奉美國遠東海軍艦隊總司令馬克威之命、馳往視察、昨已抵肇事地點、美法瑞典西班牙希臘等國政、得均電弔溺斃士兵、

自由談

一得之言 224

— 李龍

愛克司光如能照見人心。世間惡人。必被淘汰凈盡。

無風起浪。惟情海中有之

遠親不如近鄰一句話。在上海地方是不合用的。因爲上海地方的鄰舍。大都不相識。也相識不得的。

將要自殺的人。倘能想到死且不怕。尙有何事可怕。也許能積極的做

一番事業哩。

一個人的思想。太鈍了果然不好。但是過敏了也有害處。

以誠待人。縱得不到對方的好感。也不會使人懷恨。

現在的靑年男女。祇知求偶而不知擇偶。所以成功的少而失敗的多。

世間惟慈母愛子之心。最爲眞切。但世人不到絶境。决不會相着慈母之恩。

惟聰明的男女。才能利用愛情二字。爲騙錢獵艶的工具。故爲愛情而犠牲者。都是笨伯。

病從口入。禍從口出。故古人有守口若瓶之喩。

拜觀大寳記 225

— 柯定盡

日昨午後。老友王一鳴見記。偕來者三人。謂來自湘江。蓋不安於故鄉匪擾。相率來海上。以謀安居。並出定武眞蹟蘭亭集序。曩見桑世昌蘭亭考。中有「唐文皇得蘭亭眞蹟。刻之學士院。朱梁纂竊。輦置汴都。耶律德黨破石晋。此刻渡河。帝羓旣歸。與輜重棄之殺虎林。後置之定州州治。遂日定本。世稱定武蘭亭。因定州唐時置義武軍。宋避太宗諱。改名定武故也。寗和中。詔宣定武校衙舊人。問蘭亭石。輾轉得之於長安帥薛嗣昌處。時内侍梁師成爲長安承受官。批旨取舊刻。嗣昌倉卒以紙三幅作一重撫石。第一本墨深。第二本墨淺。第三生又加淺。世謂之蟬翼本：：」云云。又庚子銷夏記。亦有「孫承澤亦謂世所傳定武本有肥瘦二種：」云云。余今年見者。卷長數丈。字跡朗然。斷其爲定武眞本無疑。當時修褉之羣賢。亦於卷上繪出。神采奕奕。工細絶倫。並各系小傳。備極典麗。洵爲世間不易多覯之神品也。黃庭堅橫卷。生龍活虎。氣足神完。余友蒙翁壽芝。喜作山谷書品。近有「妙法蓮華經」書行。筆力遒勁。足與山谷媲美。右任跋中。有「山谷再世亦當首肯」之語。誠非過譽。是卷蒙翁得見。當爲怡然稱快也。淸代何紹基曾國藩等所書屏條四幅。乾隆間第一人及第之王偉人「秋水泛金鵝」立軸。並皆佳妙。與商鼎同時出土之古盤一事。式如舊時銅盆。雖中有破孔。叩之。則鏘然作金聲。斯爲可異。（商鼎已爲某洋行購去價値二萬餘金云）間有刀痕。燦燦若黃金。殊炫人目。不知其究爲何代物也。唐之靑銅鏡。惜已分碎爲二。據云人臨高處。向此鏡斜視。能觀數十里外之景物。毫釐不爽。鏡面綠花斑駁。色澤雅樸。一古代之望遠鏡也、暈紅脂玉一方。狀若龜甲而小。對光視之。中有松葉顯然。仿彿工整畫。品。凡此種種。誠爲稀世大寳。亟爲修書。介紹於黃賓虹張善孖二公。加以鑒評。而余無意中得拜觀一過。眼福爲無量矣。主有者。爲湘江李氏。其先人與曾國藩爲同寅友云。

誌秦山之遊 226

— 周才良

秦山爲金邑名勝地。相傳謂昔之秦始皇南遊時。曾駐蹕於此。距我鎭（張溪）約二里許。即南社巨子高吹萬先生之珂里也。毎歲値廢曆之三月朔望廿八及四月朔日。輒有農具市場之集。屆期如約而至者。無間遐邇。熙來攘往。貿易頗盛。惟過午則頓歸　寂。蓋尙沿襲古代日中爲市之舊制也。日前予適因事返里。而又恰逢今歲該市塲之最後一次。乃知機不可失。爰於晨興後。即徒步而往。行行重行行。未半小時而即逹。沿途竹籬茅舍。風景幽宜。頗足使久困於塵市者。胸襟爲之一爽。及抵山麓。則見人山人海。肩摩踵接。大有册陰道上之勢。綜計兩旁設攤凡二百餘。全山幾無隙處。視所陳列。則大抵以農具爲最多。惜仍墨守舊法。午篇一列。我國農産事業之不進步。言之可嘆。繼乃拾級而上。步行凡三折而始逹山巓。巓有一古寺。寺屋橫列僅三楹。而境頗淸曠。予迺入内稍息。坐甫定。忽覩壁上有所謂歪詩者。塗抹殆滿。雅俗雜陳。閲之殊堪發噱。此種汚衊名勝之惡習。未知昉自何人。語云。名土不値半文錢。信然。旋辭出。天忽陣雨。遂逕至山下凉亭暫避。時隨予而來者。愈聚愈衆。未幾。即告客滿。亭係新築。製有一聯云、「最惜飄蓬如過客。不堪折柳贈行人。」語意深刻。頗足使予儕過客讀之而心驚不已也。少頃雨止。而農市亦告終。予始言旋歸而爲之記。

新奇之騙術 227

— 劉夢蝶

錫之東亭鎭。有華氏者。三笑彈詞中華太師洪山之後人也。有女出嫁相去三十里之長安鎭。旣生子矣。一日下午。女見東亭人某甲岔息而至。告曰。爾父昨夜三更忽得急病。醫治不及。天明死矣。我來報喪也。女聞之大驚。一　幾絶。甲旋續言曰。爾母言。術者已定今日夜半入殮。命爾坐肩輿奔歸。所有衣包諸物。輿中不便携帶者。可先收拾交我帶回日幕途遥。速爲計也。女然其說。急向閨中摒擋諸事。念此行須留住多日。故衣履飾物備足。成一大包。旣畢。以甲向出入母家。似曾相識。不之疑也。即授之而去。俄而女倩人爲備肩輿。抱子登輿。一路掩泣而行。及抵家。天已黑。下輿入門。即縱聲大哭。聲聲呼父。父於内室聞聲。驚出問故。家人亦畢集而驚。乃女見父而驚益甚也。已而知父無恙。始拭涙而笑。轉悲爲喜。若不暇計衣包之損失也者。然父恚甚。命人徧覓某甲於市。而杳如黃鶴矣。蓋甲故紅丸黨之健者。近絶糧已三日。乃異想天開。以濟在陳之憂。然太惡作劇矣。

負氣後之成功 228

— 鷄冠

前日在友人席上。聞周君言。夫子廟附近有二食肆。望衡比字。相互作營業上之競爭。據知者道。中含一段負氣之歷史。述之亦足解頣也。

初寗人有金某者。淸晨率就食於外。某日至夫子廟某餐館進茶點。適生意鼎盛。堂倌奔走甚忙。俟一小時餘。而所呼包餕。久久不至。金不耐。盛氣質館侍。侍不爲下。亦怒目相向。且嘲之曰。若以此間招待不周。食品太遲。則祗好君自已設一餐館。始能指揮如意矣。冷語帶諷。金乃憤然離座而出。不意時越數月。隣近即聞有新肆之開張。所售揚製點食。無不相同。其主人即負氣而出之金某也。營業經年。生涯不惡。後來居上。此實受館侍一激之賜矣。

又曩聞故鄉人談。吳興城内館驛河兩岸。渡船林立。可由此之逹金婆弄及右文館前。城有溫某。家富於資。某日天雨就渡。容與中流。頗嫌遲滯。因與榜人發生口角。榜人亦不遜。譏之曰。汝欲求速。祗好在河上架橋耳。彼殆不識爲溫某。故以此難之也。其後地方上忽聞有鳩工造橋之議。主其事者。即受辱於榜人之溫某是。橋於前歲告成。題名曰苕梁。一時渡船營業。大受打擊。而行人亦稱便利。金錢萬能。此與前述殊途而同歸。無以名之。祗可目爲負氣後之成功而已。

藝訉　名畫家趙半跛吳子鼎馬萬里三君。均擅詩書畫三絶之才。尺帛寸練。得者寳之。現特於（十三日）起。聯合舉行畫展會於寗波同鄉會。爲期三日。想當有一悉盛况云（太瘦生）

束胸之檢查 229

— 陶麗亞

女子束胸之風。自盛行以來。前行後效。有進無退。雖歷經内政部遵令查禁。無如言者諄諄。聽乾藐藐。而尤以各學校女生爲最。現聞浙江蕭山縣立女子中學。以女生束胸。實屬有礙身體健康。特令各女生一律解放。并擬定期檢查。以免隱諱。故該校女生。日來莫不羞形於色云。

女子束胸之害。非但關係個人身體之康健及嫁後之生育。至深且鉅。而影響所及。足致民族於衰弱地位。今該校首創解放。消息四播。不但爲女子本身喜。更可爲民族之前途慶也。

說部扶輪會

三個時代（四） 230

— 張恨水

（二）爲窩頭犠牲

到了下午四點鐘。張小三兒是交車的時候了。把車子送到車廠子裏去。交了五十個子兒的車分。還剩下一百五十枚。也有銅子。也有銅子票。一齊揣在身上。拿五個大子。買了一盒烟捲。嘴裏啣着一根。挨着墻陰。一步慢似一步的走回去。他家是個大雜院。統共十幾間房。住了八家人家。這個大雜院的大字。不是贊這房屋大。乃是贊這院子大雜而特雜。這信家人家。除了三家拉車的而外。都是尙鞋匠趕大車揑糖人兒的一些小手藝買賣。張小三一進院子。就見他媳婦張二嫂拿着肥皂臉盆。放在屋檐下一張方凳子上。那様子是打算洗臉。他走上前。一伸脚。凳子踢翻了。臉盆噹的一聲。潑了一地的水。張二嫂正要進屋子去拿白布手巾呢。一回頭頓着脚道。「你抽瘋了嗎。臉盆碍着你什麽事。」張小三將嘴上的烟捲。抿着斜樹了起來。駡道。「拉車的媳婦。買洋胰子洗臉。美個什麽　兒。我張小三不打虎。（註。打虎者。即以妻嫁人。然後席捲而逃之騙局。）用不着你這様苦搗飾。要不然。這胡同裏那個小白臉子好。你想勾引他。」張二嫂是個黃色的柿子臉。腦後梳拖髻。宜拖到脖子上去。可是左右兩邊。都有一大仔黃頭髮。拖到耳朶邊。身上一件藍布褂子。像道袍一般。布不貼肉。伊頭一擺。兩仔亂髮和拖髻。都隨着摇擺。將那隻露出半截的黃蠟胳膞。抬將起來。指點着道。「張小三兒。你說的是人話嗎。人窮水不窮。窮得臉都不該要嗎。八個子兒買塊糙胰子洗臉。這不算過分。你捨不得這幾個子兒也成。往後我屎裏抓一把。尿裏抓一把。就這様作飯你吃。我告訴你。往後别這様發窮瘋。老娘是騎驢子翻賬本兒。走着瞧。」張小三兒將嘴裏烟捲。向地下一扔。噗哧一聲笑道。「他倒拿矯。張小三不短這様一個巧媳婦。多咱發了財。咱們是：：：」砰的一聲。屋子門關上了。張二嫂在屋子裏道。「别進來了。發財去罷。」張小三道。「别鬧。我得進去拿小衣換。我要到澡堂子裏去洗個澡。」張二嫂道。「誰和你鬧。你不到尿桶裏去照照你的臉。你也配嗎。」

黃海環遊記（二九） 231

— 黃炎培

黃海記遊六十韻

遼陽三月冰解堅。我隨春色出柳邊。遵陸不如浮海便。假途靑島趨大連。羣鷗送我思拳拳。。招鷗得句欲扣舷。故壘蟲沙十五年。摩挲氣象猶千。觀星臺成窺大圜。天地之妙在眼前。大盜入室主失權。攫取寳藏炫市塵。昔所未見今見焉。千山之下試温泉。暫滌塵襟翩欲仙。瀋陽直入摇吟鞭。佳兒佳婦迎懽然。　　大庠靑一　。晨羞夕膳聞春絃。畫入城市相周旋。仲宣記室何翩翩。江山文藻思鬱綿。徧徵文獻成巨編。白山黑水擔一肩。就中尤服賢令賢。輕車簡從行陌阡。大韓英屯古所傳。習齋訪父此涕漣。其人其地厚得天。有官愛民不愛錢。訓衆言簡理則圓。歸途訪古人廟　。昭陵石馬碧草芊。丹躉翠思不下鍵。瀋陽十日期未愆。莘莘請業日夕虔。愧乏廣長舌粲蓮。馬訾一水古朝鮮。漢山漢江名且沿。明月樓頭墨滿篷。旂亭入唱驚四筵。朝上龍頭松鎖烟。暮發馬關入不眠。櫻花滿野雪滿巓。雪膚花貎爭春妍。雷車飛渡江户川。春城花祭紛雲軿。東京西京相後先。落英轉眼聞啼鵑。蘆湖西　浮畫船。大涌谷口釜沸煎。四山一白雲蔓延。富士曾無半面緣。山靈和我各眼穿。紺衣吾婦空足胼。碧海雞豚肥可憐。金閣古寺路迴邅。長崎一棹歸思牽。收拾遊程復硯田。成此環遊黃海篇。（完）

商業新聞

金融標金蘊伏軟勢 232

起伏祇三四兩昨十二日標金續濳跌勢、稍有波折、終日徘徊於八百兩内外、惟風浪不大、而盤頭不過三四兩、統市有九兩零迥顧、結果已跌五兩之譜、至銀市報升初開略降、旋後因傳說六月十五日美國銀市交易所行將開幕、猶恐滬上投機商往購銀條、乃價或被上漲、故人心趨下、致金價驟然敲破八百兩、至外匯明暗均萎、復已掛長半檔、櫃面上買賣不等、至午時匯票似轉和緩、復已透出八百兩之外、後市尙平、略有進退、最後計爲八百零二三兩、而同業意志惝恍、紛異莫測云云、

晨收前發現瀉象自早間七月開盤小去一兩、爲八百零六兩二錢、蓋大條回長十六分之一、銀價八分之一、私電只升十六分之一、洵爲美國尙無賣意、旋後元春元茂永丙興等均有賣出、故又跌去四兩、九點一刻爲零二兩二錢、至於英金由華銀行賣與英日等行八月份二五、旣而大連帮及物品套頭等買進、並由華義吃去下月英金二五、遂又提起一兩零、先令揭佈時爲零三兩四錢、惟掛牌放是一二五、美金二五、日金小去一分半、且由元興永大興永餘大乾昌祥源成等出售、即行貶落三兩餘、將至十點爲七百九十九兩四錢、其間計有一兩餘高下、倐忽間恒興乾昌祥等來進、即已加至八百零一兩八錢、入後台灣出大連一兩七錢零八七五、又英金銀行買去三一二五、繼則難賣、益以志豐永恒餘元春益餘信亨等傾向賣出、急轉下風、一落四兩數錢、至十點半猝爲七百九十七兩一錢、俄而投機商吳某及乾昌祥元亨丙興萬興順利等咸進、又銀行吃進英金二五、至十一點爲八百零三兩、轉瞬退至八百兩零零五錢、復由元豐永恒餘等買進、而各號曾結英金計一八七五至二五、市面見好、至十一點三刻爲八百零三兩八錢、萬興同太昌等脫手、迨午刻爲零二兩七錢、旋又抑至一兩三四錢、揭價改爲八百三十八兩二錢、抑小三十五六兩至四十兩外、午收三十五六兩、

後市稍有徘徊後市開盤零二兩二錢、繼爲三兩、印匯近期低而遠期升、故即爲零一兩七錢、大興永等來進、忽已加至零三兩二錢、往後物品及永豐福昌等傾售、良以英金可結二五、人心一挫、遂降四兩餘、至三點後爲七百九十九兩、惟間有一二兩興伏、以後正金吃英金二五至二一二五、並以元茂永元成永福餘元興永等皆已爭購、乃價漸漲四兩、然有一兩餘盤旋、直至四點零爲零三兩二錢、此時印匯亦報小一安那、嗣後稍有數錢上落、似濳小勢、迨四點三十分收市爲零二兩四錢、比較前日計跌四兩八錢、後又做至二兩零、按前後市最大價八百零六兩三錢、最小價七百九十七兩一錢、相差九兩二錢、物品早市六兩二錢、午收二兩八錢、下午二兩半、收市二兩二錢、揭價計撳三十五六兩、登賬八百零三兩、補水零一兩、下午八百兩、

各號交易紛異計乾昌祥·萃昌永·恒興·元茂永·元亨·宏利·福餘·源茂·丙興均進、萬興·順利求過於供、志豐永·大德成·福泰·元興永·福太亨·益餘·源成乍出乍進、同太昌·大興永·元太永·福昌·元春均有出售、信亨售了一千多條、下午元茂永·乾昌祥·元大永·宏利·福餘·元興永·大興永·元成永·福太亨均進、元亨·恒興亦進、永豐·福昌志豐永并物品·萬興·同太昌均售、源泰·大德成·恒餘·義豐永出納不一、大連帮共核買進一千餘條、廣帮只進四五百條、投機商吳某略進云、

外匯市尙平定 233

昨英美印銀市、均已報升、而匯兌則降、殆匯豐各匯均已掛長半檔、計英金一二五、計爲一先令二便士、美金二五、計二十八元三七五、日金跌一分半、爲一兩七錢四分、其他均亦放長、至於内盤初平後鬆、午時回平、下午由萎復平、惟金市續跌、而匯市尙可站定、迨結果均與前晚不相上下、惟聞紐約銀子交易所、將已成立、乃銀條或能起色耶、昨天華商交易尙屬活動、計英金約成交二十餘萬鎊、金業中大致出多結少、統核抛出十餘萬鎊、日商銀行如正金三井買意不倦、又美金少數抛出、而日金由大連帮等結進大連票一百萬元之譜云、

滬南昨日米情裏路到頭二十餘艘、北粳去化極呆、價跌二角、蘇同北㘮白粳亦趨下游、情况列劣、全市城鄉走銷竟淡、行情復修尺半、南帮·石浦·泗涇·松江等薄稻早稻、跌風轉沉、用去二三角之鉅、實緣買氣寂寞、到頭接抵、産地告軟所致也、洋杜尖來貨雖略轉稀、乃積者欠化、寗胃仍閉、本街仍屬微細、致價續短半尺、糯米白陰銷亦轉淡、形勢下游、

標粉步開步降 241

昨日粉市、上下午開盤後、各月份市面、均趨逐步銳落之象、以洋麥之報價、又小一二三角左右不等、天時又風和日麗、良好異常、國内外之環境、旣利於空頭、内地帮之心思、彷彿亦不能不無動於中、手中之多頭籌碼、祇好逐步回出、雖廠家依然擯守、南洋帮略有收進、然大勢所趨、終於低落不已、因江南北之新麥、就最近言、已有七成以上之收獲、様品寄申、均屬乾燥異常、江北一帶、且較往年爲優、市氣之不振、縱非人力所能左右也、結果本月份較前日跌二分七厘半、七月份跌二分半、八月份跌一分半、九月跌一分七厘半、十月份跌一分二厘半、十一月份跌一分七厘半云、

期麥一致疲極 242

洋米續有售開 243

— 顧昻若譯

「英法美軍各總司令繼續指揮其部隊、各總司令如以福煦將軍的訓令致使其部隊處於危險地位有權向本國政府申訴、」

勞合喬治君從倫敦前來出席、在百龍上岸驅車到蒲伐亞、克萊孟梭君已先到、喬治君在途中遇着向後撤退的英軍、他見軍容不振軍心渙散、知道形勢不佳、因此他帶了沮喪的印象到會甚遲、

不過他不久就擺脫了這頺唐的神氣而恢復了他回來奮發有爲的特性、他在會議席上他對我聲明道一英國人民對君信任、你被推爲聯軍總司令在我國裏一致歡迎、」

散了會我們離室而去、他以慣常愉快的態度對我說、「現在我賭何人、羅登獨夫呢、還是福煦呢、」我泰然自若的回答他道、「你先得做我的後盾你就贏了、因爲羅登獨夫必須攻破我軍、現在他無能爲力了、至於我們呢、我軍現在的任務就在阻止他、關於此點我們很有把握、以後我們到了時機攻破他、｜那是另一問題、我們能做到怎様地步、不久就見分曉了、」

蒲伐亞恊定不能完全容納我的建議、因此未能把我的職權擴充到節制自北海以至亞德里亞海西綫的全綫、或在那裏作戰的全部聯軍、不過它已經包含指揮法綫戰事的要素、法綫是主要戰區、作戰的美英法軍也是聯軍的主力軍隊、但克萊阵梭君現已得着英美政府贊成這新方案、他一定寗願先把聯軍總司令的權力限止在這戰區及這三部軍隊、以待時機的成熟、這結果一旦獲得、他保留着圖謀將來擴充恊定的可能到包括意大利戰區、一面及到比軍、一面及到意軍、

意國加入的動議、最高戰事評議會曾於五月二日在亞伯費加以研究、翁倫多君及宋尼拿君、以意政府的名義、宣稱、不能無條件的贊同蒲伐協定、但他們爲妥洽起見、主張把意綫及意軍的指揮加以區别、這方案經其他政府同意、内容如下、

㈠意綫從現在起依照杜倫恊定歸福煦將軍節制、

㈡至於意軍、須俟别國聯軍至阿爾帕斯山外在他指揮之下如在法境同様形勢中作戰的時候、始歸其節制、

意政府這様的限制仍使聯軍總司令有權巡視意綫、到必要的時候且可利用橫跨亞爾帕斯山戰區的可能實行其戰略

關於比軍部分、最高戰事評議會於七月三日在凡爾賽討論這個問題、當時聯軍準備在法境採取攻勢、預計要把比軍參加這次戰事、最好把他們同别國聯軍一様歸我節制、但比軍參謀長紀倫少將引據比國的憲法正式反對此議、因未能成立諒解、

實則這種不妥洽的態度大半發生於原則上面、並不是一成不變的、幾星期後、比王絶不猶豫的接受依據聨軍總司令的調度指揮比法英美聯軍在法蘭作戰的任務、

五月二日、協約國政府議决取銷三月前成立的執行委員會、因現在無此必要了、五月十四日、我接着法境聯軍總司令的稱號、

但這不過是在紙上規定我的職權的正式手續、實際上這様産生的聯軍總司令如何行施職權尙待分曉、

一九一八年四月初、形勢仍舊岌岌可危、戰綫因敵人的屢次勝利而展期、要以力竭聲嘶的士卒挽回頺勢、不可再事磋砣了、

在他方面、貝當將軍把第五軍沿着亞眠更向北開進、這支軍隊因爲當時不想採取攻勢、因從後備軍抽調補充、他且把疴阿斯軍圑向西調動、這軍圑有兩師之衆、其中一部分向疴阿斯河右岸前進、他更把第一騎兵圑從安逹里調到奥美爾、

福悅將軍奉令立刻調動左翼的後備軍、以備在逼切的時候在魯斯沙姆戰區援助英國第四軍、

末了、訓令第十軍司令梅斯特將軍處置阿拉斯前敵的軍事、如其敵軍進攻、則主要的防綫務必全力固守、作戰的步驟、訓令裏爲他及第三軍統統規定好的、他開頭的佈置和他參戰的方法也給他指明的、

佈置法軍在阿拉斯與沙姆河之間參戰的時候、我也注意到盡力援助英軍總司令、因他給法蘭特戰爭的物質的及精神的困難弄得心神不寗、十二日我决定把兩天前已開始供給他的援兵增加、

我因令奥美爾區域的後備隊、第二騎兵圑向聖亞美開拔、十三日開到之後、準備會合法軍百三十三師增援英國第二軍、

第二騎兵圑司令羅皮育將軍來到沙格斯（註、我的司令部自四月七日已遷移到沙格斯、在格蘭費邑的西北三哩、）請訓、爲他指示作戰的任務的時候、我特别吩咐他竭力維持英國第一第二軍間的連絡、

戰略的大綱如下、

㈠全力支持罅口的兩翼、在北面繼續的佔據克末爾加賽爾山之綫、向南、在南面繼續的佔據倍塞内聖亞美之綫、向東北、

㈡在這固守的兩翼之間、向東佔領各要點阻敵前進、

（未完）

靑年園地

復旦劇社公演說謊者 267

日期　定今明兩日

地點　寗波同鄉會

復旦劇社自上屆公演「西哈諾」後、即籌備第十一次大公演、劇本係英國喜劇家瓊斯名作「說謊者」、已於本月一日晚在復旦大學一度公演、茲擇定今明兩日、假寗波同鄉會作盛大之貢獻、此劇經該社改譯、故極適合國情、全無空氣不調和之缺陷、加之佈景設計、矞皇典麗、劇中情節、滑稽幽默、演員精選、均屬富於舞臺經騐者、聞門券代售處爲四馬路北新、光華、現代三書局、座價爲半元一元云、

復旦的「說謊者」 268

— 悟

「近來上海的戲劇空氣沉寂極了」

在這三百萬人的大都會裏呼吸着的人們、誰都這様感到的吧、眞的、南國劇社、瓦解了、戲劇協社、不見有排演的消息、辛酉劇團、從表現過所謂難劇運動以來彷彿没有了努力的意思、摩登劇社、曾一度努力流動劇塲運動的也已經各溫各的好夢、停止了進行的工作、可是各種學校劇社、在十九年的所謂戲劇的年頭曾經風起雲湧接踵的活動過來、而今年來、也跟出版界的狂颷潮一稱地消沈、没落了、

然而、上海的愛美劇團、未見得一概汨没的吧、像最近成立的菁莪劇社、素霓劇社、不是紛紛預備着公演嗎、

復旦劇社、曾經接連地努力過十次的出演、對於　　着的中國戲劇界有過不少的貢獻、而且上年曾努力過在中國劇圑中不敢出演的、須有五六十人登台的偉大的「西哈諾」、現在、再扯志了大　、排練第十一次的出演、

這次出演的劇本、便是英國偉大的喜劇家瓊斯的傑作「說謊者」、「說謊者」、過去、是轟動過歐美的劇界、博到不少的佳評的、

著者、在劇中大聲疾呼一個人爲了一女子而犠牲其榮、名譽、國家責任、良心、以及一切於不顧、何等不値得呀、這在我國、正有不少爲迷戀女子而放棄民族國家的危難於不顧的人們、該是當頭的一大棒喝、

作爲人生的喜劇的「說謊者」、是諷剌當時英國兩性間的婚姻糾紛、是指點入了迷的男男女女、現在由該社朱端鈞先生改譯一過、使適合中國的國情、

劇中叙述一個南洋富商、偶然來上海遊玩、認識了幾個有丈夫的女性、而和其中最漂亮的一個陷在瘋狂一般的戀愛的怒潮中。這様的開頭、於是變化出一段又滑稽又幽默又深刻、又有人生意義的故事、

不意、那一對戀人碰巧在吳淞海濱旅館會晤、碰巧又給那女的丈夫的弟弟撞見、這如何得了、旅館幽會的罪名接着加在他們倆的肩上、由這様的誤會、於是最有趣味、也是全劇最緊要的關頭的第三幕展開了、

無可奈何的他們、跟自已的親戚朋友商量了、如何在自家的丈夫面前掩飾呢、說眞話告訴給他聽嗎、這様事情一定會越鬧越大的、决定了、造一個圓滿的謊吧、少數人商定的謊語、一步步、給大部分的人參加了、居然有三錮男性和三個女性共同圓謊、而逹到全劇最精彩的一刻、可是不幸、因爲人多口雜、預料以爲圓滿的謊語不意露了破綻、差不多鬧到不可收拾、

故事在這裏轉過來了、從快將破裂的一對夫妻、折到重溫舊好的路而結束、在末一幕、有幾句名言可以奉告正在離婚熱的空氣中度着悲慘生活的男女們的　　「你不要以爲你結了婚、就可以放下你的妻子不去理她了、不能的、你現在娶了一位上海最漂亮的女子、可是假使你不繼續跟她依然戀愛下去、别的人要要跟她戀愛了呢、没有話說的這是人生的悲劇、」

這一本劇中、有六位女士登台、破了列次各劇圑公演時需要女演員之多的例、如果將舞台換在國貨商塲、也許有人將以爲是時裝展覧會了哩、然而不是的、她們都是愛好戲劇同時頗願意爲戲劇努力的女靑年、

她們、這幾位女演員、是一般人口頭上所常之稱揚的東宮中的漂亮公主、最最美麗的公主呢、儘收集在這劇本中、如果需要預先介紹一番的話、也不妨略略說一說的、

該最先提起的、是梁培樹女士、她富於演劇的天才、無須說得的、表情的細膩、說白的明亮等等、已經有了定評、原來她曾充演偉大的西哈諾中的女主角哩、這一次、富於熱情的女主角是

李蓮女士、她呀、不錯的、表演的技巧很熟練、舞台的經騐非凡充足、她紛演過的角色不少啦、不愧爲名導演家手下訓練出來的一員、還有她的妺妺

琴荃女士、也是新劇界女演員中的人才、扮演解色的輕重不在乎、正是學習着在成功的中途、此番劇中須要幽嫻的性格的是

歐陽女士、她正和劇中的那個性相稱、唱的一口好歌、在對話中時、聽了、如嚦嚦鶯聲鳥語、

其他的幾位女士、想不能一一的介紹、總之都是話劇界中顯過頭角來的、因爲這劇中有這様多的女性、所以劇的題名曾一度改爲「說謊的女人們、」

如果竭望着想一見這幾位女士和這巧妙的劇情的、巧得很、今天就　波同鄉會公演了、公演云、

「說謊者」要角梁培樹女士 269

— 冰攝

1931.06.13

Orders 1

The National Government, on the 12th, issued an order appointing Li Yizi, Ying Zhenfu, and Ma Jidi as Councillors of the Military Council. This order. Another order granted Li Ming, Huo Kuizhang, Li Moan, and Wu Liangchen the Fourth Class Precious Tripod Medal. This order. Another order approved the recommendation from Chiang Kai-shek, concurrently President of the Executive Yuan, as reported by He Yingqin, Minister of Military Affairs, that Xu Gongdian, Secretary; Chen Binru, Zhang KuiSu, clerks of the General Affairs Office; Cai Fusheng, clerk of the Ordnance Department of the Military Supply Bureau; Wang Jian, technician of the Ordnance Bureau, etc., be reassigned; that Li Shengfu, clerk of the Ordnance Department of the Army Department; Yang Liufeng, secretary of the Ordnance Bureau; Chen Yunsheng, technician, etc., be permitted to resign upon request; and that Shen Fen, clerk of the General Affairs Office; Ma Xiang, clerk of the Aviation Administration; Wu Zhengeng, senior technician of the Construction Department of the Military Supply Bureau; Wu Kaiyao, clerk; Xuan Jie, adjutant; Li Guodian, clerk of the Ordnance Bureau, etc., be relieved of their duties as they have been reassigned. This order. Another order approved the recommendation from Chiang Kai-shek, concurrently President of the Executive Yuan, as reported by He Yingqin, Minister of Military Affairs, to appoint Huang Xun as clerk of the General Affairs Office of the Ministry of Military Affairs; Shen Fen as clerk of the General Affairs Department of the Army Department of the Ministry of Military Affairs; Sun Xuebin as clerk of the Ordnance Department of the Army Department of the Ministry of Military Affairs; Xia Yixun as senior technician of the Construction Department of the Military Supply Bureau; Xuan Jie as clerk of the Construction Bureau of the Military Supply Bureau; Duanmu Dang as adjutant of the Construction Department of the Military Supply Bureau; Yu Yizu as secretary of the Ordnance Bureau of the Ministry of Military Affairs; Zhu Wenbo as clerk of the Ordnance Bureau of the Ministry of Military Affairs; Zhou Xiuzhai, Wu Zengqi, Jin Yulin, and Hu Zongpu as technicians of the Ordnance Bureau of the Ministry of Military Affairs. This order.

Domestic Important Telegrams

The Fifth Plenary Session Will Be Approved to Convene Today 2

Twenty-One Central Committee Members Already in Nanjing

(Nanjing) The Fifth Plenary Session is scheduled to hold its opening ceremony at 8 a.m. on the 13th at the Central Party Headquarters. The order of proceedings has been drafted by the Central Secretariat, and a summary is as follows: (1) Central Committee members take their seats; (2) Play music; (3) Sing the Party song; (4) Bow three times to the Party and national flags, and the portrait of the late Premier; (5) The chairman respectfully reads the Premier's will; (6) Observe three minutes of silence; (7) The chairman delivers the opening address; (8) Play music; (9) Take a photograph; (10) Ceremony concludes. In addition, the Party Headquarters' decorations have been completed by the General Affairs Section. Two celebratory arches have been erected at both the main and second entrances. The horizontal inscription at the main entrance reads "Unify the Will, Unite the Spirit," and the couplet reads "Abide by the Provisional Constitution during the Period of Political Tutelage, Strive for Long-Term Peace and Stability of the Republic of China." The horizontal inscription at the second entrance reads "Opening Ceremony of the Fifth Plenary Session of the Third Central Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang," and the couplet reads "Consolidate Unity, Ensure Peace." The horizontal inscription in the auditorium reads "Spirit of Fraternity," and the couplet reads "Implement the Resolutions of the National Assembly, Strive for National Reconstruction during the Period of Political Tutelage." Other areas are also decorated with colorful flowers, creating a completely renewed atmosphere. (12th Special Dispatch).

(Nanjing) The greatest purpose of the Fifth Plenary Session is to accept the resolutions of the National Assembly, determine the date for the Fourth National Congress, and, in accordance with the Provisional Constitution, amend the Organic Law of the National Government. At the same time, all heads of Yuan, Ministries, and Commissions will be reappointed according to law. Furthermore, there will be expressions of commendation for Chiang's devoted attitude towards suppressing the bandits. It is said that there are not many proposals from the Central Committee members, as the resolutions of the National Assembly are already the crystallization of national public opinion, and only diligent implementation is needed to benefit the people and enrich the nation. Even the few proposals that do exist are nothing more than matters concerning the advancement of Party affairs. (12th Special Dispatch).

(Nanjing) The legal quorum for the Fifth Plenary Session is 19 people. There are already 21 people in Nanjing, so there is no problem for the meeting to be held tomorrow. Chiang plans to leave Nanjing on the 16th, or possibly go to Lushan on the 18th. (12th Special Dispatch).

(Nanjing) Zhang Zhijiang and Ye Chucang arrived in Nanjing at the same time on the 11th. Ye is attending the Fifth Plenary Session, while Zhang is seeking instructions regarding pacification matters. (12th Special Dispatch).

(Nanjing) Yang Shuzhuang, Song Ziwen, Cai Yuanpei, and Wu Tiecheng are all scheduled to arrive in Nanjing on the morning of the 13th to attend the Fifth Plenary Session. (12th Special Dispatch).

(Nanjing) He Yingqin sent a telegram to Wang Boqun on the 11th stating that if the quorum is met for the Fifth Plenary Session, he will not enter Nanjing for the time being, so as to dedicate himself to military affairs. If one or two people are still lacking, he himself will fly to Nanjing to attend. (12th Special Dispatch).

Commander-in-Chief Chiang's Headquarters to Be Established in Nanchang 3

Personnel of the Political Training Department Departed Yesterday

(Nanjing) Commander-in-Chief Chiang's headquarters will be established in Nanchang. At the same time, preparations are being made in Lushan for Chiang's rest and recuperation. It is said that Chiang may depart around the 17th. (12th Special Dispatch).

(Nanjing) Personnel from the Political Training Department, who are accompanying Chiang on his trip to Jiangxi, departed tonight, led by Zhou Fo Hai, to Xiaguan, to wait for the ship to sail to Jiangxi, along with 30 boxes of propaganda material for suppressing the communists, which will also be transported to Jiangxi. (12th Special Dispatch).

(Nanjing) With Chiang's departure for Hubei and Jiangxi imminent, the first batch of aides will depart on the afternoon of the 13th, taking the Changxing and Yongxing ships to Jiangxi. As for the second batch of important aides, they will travel with Chiang. (12th Special Dispatch).

Victory at the Front in Jiangxi Province 4

Chiang Cables He Yingqin to Commend Him

(Nanjing) Chiang sent a telegram to He Yingqin this morning, roughly stating that the front had achieved victory, that Jiang and Cai had rendered meritorious service, and that the victory at Nanfeng, where Mao's forces were located, clearly demonstrated excellent command and control, and so on. (13th/11th Special Dispatch).

(Nanjing) Jiangxi telegram reports that the Communist bandits in Yudu, Ruijin, etc., are experiencing internal strife, with the cadre faction disarming the Trotskyist faction, confiscating over 2,000 firearms. (12th Special Dispatch).

Headquarters Newly Forms Two Committees for Party and Political Affairs 5

Cheng Tianfang and Cao Haosen Appointed Chairmen

(Nanjing) The headquarters plans to newly form a Party Affairs Committee, divided into five sections: Secretariat, Organization, Training, Propaganda, and Evaluation; and a Political Committee, divided into four sections: Local Autonomy, Disaster Relief, Secretariat, and Inspection. Currently, the Chairman of the Jiangxi Party Committee will be assumed by Cheng Tianfang, a member of the Central Committee. The Chairman of the Political Committee will be Cao Haosen, the Vice Minister of Military Administration. It is said that the members of the two committees have been internally determined, with Shao Lizi, Zhou Fo Hai, Yang Yongtai, Xiong Shihui, Lu Disheng, and over twenty others being appointed to various positions.

Wan Fulin Invites Shi Yousan to Come to Beiping 6

Deputy Headquarters Allocates Provisions to Shi's Troops

Shi and Sun Recently Deeply Realized Their Errors

(Beiping) Wan Fulin telegraphed Shi Yousan today, earnestly inviting him to come to Beiping to meet and dispel rumors. Shi has recovered from his illness and has moved back to his private residence from the American Hospital in Shun De. (11th Special Dispatch).

(Beiping) Bi Guangyuan visited Wan Fulin this morning to report on Shi Yousan's recent situation. (12th Special Dispatch).

(Beiping) The Deputy Headquarters has now allocated food expenses for the soldiers of Shi Yousan's troops, which have been received by the responsible personnel of Shi's troops. (12th Special Dispatch).

(Beiping) Liu Weiyong, a member of the inspection committee for Shi Yousan's troops, and Bi Guangyuan, Shi's representative in Beiping, returned to Beiping today to report to Zhang Xueliang on the inspection situation of Shi's troops and their current deployment. (11th Special Dispatch).

(Beiping) Xiong Bin went to Shunde last night to convey Chiang Kai-shek's message of comfort to Shi Yousan's troops. (12th Special Dispatch).

(Beiping) A certain important figure in the Northeast told reporters that the rumors about the situation in North China are: (1) the Deputy Commander is ill; (2) the problem of Shi Yousan and Sun Dianying. The Deputy Commander's illness has reached the convalescent stage, proving that the rumors spread by outsiders are inaccurate. Shi and Sun have recently deeply realized their errors, and have repeatedly telegraphed the Central Government expressing their complete obedience. The rumors that the Central Government will transfer Shi and Sun to Gansu are not true. (12th Special Dispatch).

(Beiping) Wan Fulin telegraphed urging Shi Yousan to come to Beiping. Wan will return to Heilongjiang after meeting with Shi. (12th Special Dispatch).

(Beiping) Bi Guangyuan said that when he visited Wan Fulin this morning, he expressed that Shi Yousan absolutely obeys the Central Government and the Deputy Commander. Wan said that the Central Government and the Deputy Commander have never discriminated against Shi's troops, and that he can guarantee the maintenance of military pay. Chiang sent a telegram to Shi Yousan and Sun Dianying, hoping that they would maintain peace and unity and return to the right track. The telegram was over 3,000 words long. Shi Yousan sent a telegram to Wan Fulin, saying that he is clear about the overall situation, has realized his errors, and that the North can be pacified. (12th Special Dispatch).

(Beiping) A certain important figure said that Shi Yousan and Sun Dianying absolutely obey the Central Government. Shi is expected to come to Beiping within days. Shao Lizi's trip to Jinan had no mediation mission. The rumors that the Central Government will transfer Shi and Sun to Gansu are even more untrue. (12th Central News Agency Dispatch).

(Jinan) Cheng Xixian, Shi Yousan's representative, visited Shao Lizi, Jiang Bocheng, and Han Fuqu today, claiming that Shi was greatly moved by Chiang's address to the officers and soldiers, absolutely believes in the Central Government, obeys the Central Government, and that there will be no troop movements. Furthermore, Xiao Zhenying and Liu Ruzhou went to Nanjing to represent Shi Yousan in seeking instructions from Chiang. (12th Special Dispatch).

Aviation Class Training Aircraft Crashes at Military Academy 10

Aircraft Falls on Zhongshan Road

Pilot Fortunately Not Seriously Injured

(Nanjing) A student named Wang from the Aviation Class of the Central Military Academy, at 4 p.m. on the 12th, was piloting a training aircraft and took off from Ming Palace Airport for practice. Due to internal mechanical problems, the engine suddenly stopped, and the aircraft crashed near the entrance of the Central Hospital on Zhongshan Road from a height of about 40 feet above the ground, with the wings facing downwards. The engine and wings were damaged. Although the pilot was slightly shaken, he was fortunate not to be seriously injured. The aircraft was transported to the repair shop for repairs. (12th Special Dispatch).

The World Commercial Savings Bank: Aiding the Cause of Education 12

Initiated by: A group of shareholders with a passion for education and extensive banking experience

Purpose: To allocate a portion of the shareholders' dividends to subsidize education for the poor.

Registered with: License granted by the Ministry of Finance of the National Government; Registration approved by the Ministry of Industry

Began operations on June 3rd

Interest Plus Gifts Available Before the End of June

The flourishing state of the Shanghai financial sector in recent years is unprecedented. However, a bank dedicated to the cause of education has been lacking. Recently, a group of shareholders from the World Book Company, who are passionate about education and have extensive banking experience, organized the World Commercial Savings Bank in Shanghai. Their highest aspiration is to use a portion of the bank's annual profits, specifically ten percent of the fifty percent of dividends designated for shareholders in the articles of association, to subsidize education for the poor. License No. 61 from the Ministry of Finance has long been granted, and the registration with the Ministry of Industry has also been approved. The head office is located in World Lane on Fourth Ma Road in Shanghai. It officially opened for business on the 3rd of this month and has quickly gained a reputation both domestically and internationally. Its operations are divided into two sections: commercial and savings. The commercial section includes: (1) commercial time deposits, with terms ranging from three months to ten years; (2) commercial demand deposits; (3) commercial current accounts; (4) overdraft facilities, all of which can be withdrawn at any time. The savings section includes: (1) demand savings deposits; (2) lump-sum deposit and withdrawal savings, with terms ranging from one to fifteen years; (3) ordinary fixed-deposit savings, with terms ranging from one to fifteen years; (4) special fixed-deposit savings, with terms ranging from one to fifteen years; (5) lump-sum deposit and installment withdrawal savings, with terms ranging from one to fifteen years; (6) periodic interest payment savings, with terms ranging from one to ten years; (7) principal-and-interest savings, with a uniform term of seven full years. The interest rates offered are higher than those of other institutions. For example, demand savings deposits offer a weekly interest rate of seven percent, calculated every six months, with interest accruing on interest. Furthermore, lump-sum deposit and withdrawal savings offer weekly interest rates ranging from 9.5 percent to 1.2 percent, which is unmatched by other savings institutions. Recognizing the difficulties of general social life, the bank has also designed various savings methods to encourage people to quickly realize the importance of savings as a safeguard for their future. For example, under the fixed-deposit savings category, if you wish to obtain a retirement fund of 10,000 yuan in the future, and you deposit for a term of fifteen years, you only need to deposit 19.3 yuan per month, and you can withdraw 10,000 yuan upon maturity. If you deposit for a term of ten years, you need to deposit 44.6 yuan per month, and you will also get 10,000 yuan upon maturity. Under the lump-sum deposit and withdrawal savings category, if you deposit 1,826.96 yuan at once for a term of fifteen years, you can also get 10,000 yuan. Under lump-sum deposit and withdrawal savings category B, if you deposit 100 yuan today for a term of fifteen years, you can get 562.35 yuan. If you deposit 5,000 yuan today for a term of ten years, you can get 14,697.15 yuan; in fifteen years, you can get a huge sum of 28,117.7 yuan. Either accumulating small amounts into large sums, which is easy and convenient, or depositing only once, which is simple and straightforward, is invariably beneficial. This is truly a great contribution to the benefit of the people. Detailed rules are available in a special chapter and can be requested at any time. Furthermore, it is reported that before the end of June, as a celebration of the opening, all savings deposited during this period will either receive an additional one percent interest, or receive book vouchers from the World Book Company, or various exquisite gifts, commemorative albums, etc., to stimulate the interest of savers. With such unique dedication to serving society, it is no wonder that the bank has won the admiration and praise of the majority of people. A1234

Current Commentary

Uchida Succeeds Senju as President of the South Manchuria Railway 13

Tokyo dispatch today. Senju, the president of the South Manchuria Railway, has resigned. The cabinet, considering the importance of this position in relation to China, decided to appoint Uchida Kosai, who previously served as Foreign Minister, Acting Prime Minister, and Ambassador to China, to succeed him. This is also something that our countrymen should pay close attention to.

The South Manchuria Railway is the most important outstanding issue in Sino-Japanese negotiations. Today, Chinese and Japanese commissioners are about to begin discussions in the Northeast. The Japanese side considers this conference to be crucial to Japan's rights in China. Furthermore, in light of China's advocacy for the abolition of unequal treaties, and intimidated by the promotion of railway networks in other countries, they are exhibiting signs of paranoia and vehemently resisting. Judging from the recent declaration of the "Overseas Comrades Association," they are determined to strengthen their stance on railway issues and take urgent measures to protect other rights and interests. Many prominent figures from the Japanese government and public sectors are listed as initiators, including several dukes and barons, indicating that the Japanese are deliberately planning to firmly defend their so-called vested rights in the South Manchuria Railway, which is undeniable. It is said that Uchida's succession as president was recommended by Prime Minister Wakatsuki, respecting the opinion of Prince Saionji. In other words, it respects the railway policy of senior statesmen in general. Although Uchida is known as a non-partisan, he is still an old-fashioned figure, and his thoughts and policies will not easily change. Although his tenure as Ambassador to China was some time ago, the Chinese people still remember Japan's foreign policy towards China at that time. Now, entrusting the important task of the South Manchuria Railway to a diplomat from the past era, if he caters to the temporary frenzy of the Japanese people, forgets that the world should be equal, insists on his consistent policies and proceeds forcefully, then the railway negotiations in the Northeast in the future will be even more difficult to be optimistic about.

Domestic Important Telegrams II

Ministry of Finance Decides to Establish a National Anti-Opium Bureau 14

Li Jihong to be the Director

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance has decided to establish a National Anti-Opium Bureau and has announced the appointment of Li Jihong as the Director. It will also establish Anti-Opium Bureaus in various provinces, directly under the control of the Anti-Opium Bureau. Organizational work is currently underway. The position of Director of the Anhui Anti-Opium Bureau has been decided to be filled by Hao Zihua. (12th Special Dispatch)

Turkey to Close Its Embassy in China 15

(Nanjing) The Turkish Embassy in China will be closed due to domestic budget cuts. Going forward, Turkey will not send envoys to China and Japan, and will entrust the Netherlands to handle all affairs related to overseas Chinese. The Turkish Chargé d'affaires, Fuat, will return home. (12th Special Dispatch)

Ministry of Finance to Send Personnel to Monitor Gold Trading 16

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance believes that the price of gold has fluctuated greatly over the past year, severely impacting the economy. The main reason for this is due to the deliberate manipulation by general speculators. It is now planned to appoint several supervisors in the gold exchange to monitor gold trading and draft provisional regulations for the supervisors consisting of thirteen articles, which will be submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval. If there is evidence of manipulation or agitation, it will be reported for strict action. (12th Special Dispatch)

Huai River Diversion Project Plan 17

(Nanjing) The Huai River Diversion Committee has decided that the project will proceed with both river and sea routes simultaneously. In order to lower the water level of Hongze Lake, the excess water will be diverted into the river and sea. However, the water level of Hongze Lake is high, and if it is discharged completely, it will inevitably dry up, which will also be detrimental to farmers' water conservancy. Currently, new-style dams and sluices will be built first, so that the water level can be freely controlled and ships can travel freely. (12th Special Dispatch)

Chiang and Cai Support the Central Government 18

(Nanjing) Jiang Guangnai and Cai Tingkai, after Chen Mingshu arrived in Ganzhou, have telegraphed to express their absolute support for the Central Government to achieve unification, and vowed to eliminate the red bandits to save the people. (12th Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The National Government Civil Affairs Department issued a circular on the 12th, forwarding Chen Mingshu's favorable telegram from Ganzhou for reference. (12th Special Dispatch)

Wang Boqun Discusses the Current Situation 19

The Situation in Guangdong Will Be Difficult to Sustain

Suppression of Bandits is Being Actively Pursued

(Nanjing) This newspaper's reporter recently visited Wang Boqun and inquired about the current situation. He kindly answered each question, which are detailed as follows:

(Question) Minister, you have been ill for a long time. Have you recovered your health? (Answer) Initially, it was a recurrence of a foot ailment, followed by typhoid fever. According to Western medical practice, I needed to rest for four weeks, so my return to Nanjing was inevitably delayed. While I was ill, it was a time of many incidents, and there was much speculation on all sides. Now that I have returned to the Ministry, the rumors have subsided.

(Question) What are your thoughts on the Guangdong incident? (Answer) I believe the Guangdong incident is a last-ditch effort of the Beiping Enlarged Conference from last year. After the Enlarged Conference failed, the reactionaries constantly sought opportunities to act. When Mr. Hu resigned, they saw it as an excellent opportunity, instigated Chen Jitang to start trouble in Guangdong. However, they were hampered by their isolation and had to contact Zhang Guijun, and further linked to groups and allies of Zhang Guijun. Recalling the past history between Wang Jingwei and Mr. Hu, and Mr. Hu's determination to oppose the Enlarged Conference last year, a small number of reactionaries actually wanted to drag him into the vortex and damage Mr. Hu's reputation, which is nothing more than a dream.

(Question) According to your observation, how will the Guangdong incident develop in the future? (Answer) The important figures in Guangdong now have different beliefs, opinions, and histories. Emotionally, they are even more of a mixture of friends and foes, so there is no reason to succeed. According to recent news, Zhang Huichang and Chen Ce have expressed their passivity. Wang Jingwei and Chen Jitang have had major disagreements over the reorganization of the Provincial Party Headquarters. After Sun Zhesheng returned the letter of appointment for the Provincial Chairmanship, although Lin Yungai replaced him, he has become discouraged due to constant constraints. Therefore, the situation in Guangdong will be difficult to sustain.

(Question) What is the Central Government's attitude towards the Guangdong affair? (Answer) As far as I know, the Central Government has always maintained an attitude of peaceful unification. However, if they ultimately do not realize their errors and are willing to be the source of trouble, then there will be corresponding preparations.

(Question) How is the suppression of bandits in Jiangxi progressing? (Answer) I have received repeated telegrams from Minister He Jingzhi. Since the Guangdong incident occurred, the red bandits have stubbornly resisted, hoping to spread their influence. However, the Central Government believes that the suppression of bandits is a matter of survival for the Chinese nation, which is even more important than the Guangdong affair. Therefore, the suppression of bandits is still being actively pursued.

(Question) There are widespread rumors that the Ministry of Transportation and the Ministry of Railways will be merged. Is this true? (Answer) This matter is within the authority of the Central Government, and due to my position, I am not in a position to express an opinion.

(Question) Minister, you recently published a notice in the newspaper about your marriage to Miss Bao. Can you tell us about the process? (Answer) In the winter of the 17th year, my first wife passed away. My mother felt that I needed someone to assist me at home, and repeatedly urged me to remarry. Relatives and friends echoed her and introduced potential candidates, one after another. I felt that traditional marriages often led to dissatisfaction, so I declined the help of relatives and friends and paid attention on my own. Miss Bao Jixin was originally a good friend, and we often interacted, so I came to know her niece, Zhi Ning. Zhi Ning is diligent in her studies and has no airs. After graduating from university last winter, my mother urged me to remarry even more urgently due to her old age and frequent illnesses. Therefore, I entrusted relatives and friends to act as matchmakers and obtained the consent of her parents, and the marriage agreement was finalized. Outside rumors that I paid a large sum to take a concubine will be proven by the facts and are not worth refuting. (12th Special Dispatch)

Central Government Plans for Suppressing Bandits 20

Committee Did Not Convene Yesterday

(Nanjing) The Central Standing Committee decided to organize a committee to plan everything for eliminating the red bandits and pacifying the local areas. A meeting was scheduled to be held at 9:00 a.m. on the 12th in the Second Meeting Hall of the Central Government. However, due to the small number of committee members who attended, it could not be convened. It will be rescheduled after Secretary-General Chen Lifu recovers from his illness. The name of the committee has not yet been determined. As for how to eliminate the red bandits in the future, it will not be announced because it is related to military affairs. (12th Special Dispatch)

The meeting was originally scheduled to be held at 5:00 p.m. on the 12th. However, since the second French representative, Mr. Gregerin, the French Consul General in Shanghai, had not yet arrived in Nanjing, the meeting was temporarily postponed to the 16th. At the same time, the first French representative, Mr. Regard, telegraphed to Shanghai, urging Gregerin to come to Nanjing to facilitate the meeting as scheduled. According to a certain gentleman, a representative from our side, the French side is indeed sincere in resolving the reorganization of the French Concession Law Court. If progress is swift, it can be resolved in two or three meetings. As for the form of resolution, it is roughly the same as the Mixed Court in the Public Concession. Regarding the name of the reorganized court, it is generally set as the Second District Court of the Shanghai Special District. At the same time, it is also planned to change the name of the Special District Court in the Public Concession to the First District Court of the Special District. (12th Special Dispatch)

Regulations on Unified Tax Treasury Bonds 23

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance has drafted regulations on short-term unified tax treasury bonds regarding the method of paying principal and interest. All bonds of 5,000 yuan and 1,000 yuan require the bondholder to have the original bond verified by the managing bank or managing office, record the principal and interest coupon, and receive the principal and interest. For bonds of 100 yuan and 10 yuan, the principal and interest coupon for that month should be detached and the principal and interest received. Regarding the method of deducting principal and interest, those who subscribe within June of the 20th year will hand over the coupon for the first period of principal and interest to the subscriber. Those who subscribe within July will detach the coupon for the first period of principal and interest, and then pay in cash, with each 100 yuan deducting the first period of principal. This will be noted on the pre-issued bond or receipt issued by the fundraising agency for separate issuance of the bond. The fundraising fee is set at one percent. Whether individuals or institutions, all those who raise funds and deposit them in the treasury will enjoy this benefit as an encouragement. However, if there are any remittance fees, etc., for depositing the funds, they must not be stipulated separately. (12th Special Dispatch)

Outer Mongolia Expands Military Preparations 25

Large Army Concentrated in the Chechen Khanate

(Peiping) According to visitors from Outer Mongolia, all political affairs and powers in Outer Mongolia have been almost entirely seized by Soviet Russia. The government organization also imitates Soviet Russia. Recently, incited by the Russians, they have expanded their military preparations and are currently concentrating their forces in the Kerulen River basin in the Chechen Khanate. They have 30,000 infantry, 40,000 cavalry, 21 aircraft, various types of over-mountain mortars and other combat supplies. The military officers are all Russians and Buriats from Uriankhai. Residents of Inner Mongolia are quite uneasy. According to a certain prince of the Ordos League, since the death of the temporary president Da Lama Tserengdondov in the eighteenth year, the Russians have long been in charge of the Mongolian army's internal direction. Recently, seeing the success of a certain country in instigating the Dalai Lama to invade Kham, they are even more eager to try. The Chechen Khanate is a vital southeast point for Outer Mongolia, connecting the eastern three provinces in the east and bordering Rehe, Chahar, and Suiyuan to the south. (Eleventh Day Special Dispatch)

(Peiping) A certain Mr. from Inner Mongolia recently arrived in Peiping and stated that the Outer Mongolian government is actively expanding its influence into Inner Mongolia. All young people from Inner Mongolia who join the service of Outer Mongolia are given important positions. They are also building four major highway trunk lines: 1) Southward from Urga (Ulaanbaatar) through Alxa to Ude, directly reaching the northern border of Zhangjiakou; 2) Northward from Maimaicheng through Kyakhta to Verkhneudinsk, reaching the border of Heilongjiang province; 3) Eastward from Urga through Kerulen to Hulunbuir, directly connecting with the Russian border; 4) Westward from Urga to Kobdo, entering Xinjiang. Furthermore, command posts have been set up in Ude, Verkhneudinsk, Hulunbuir, and Kobdo, at the border crossings between Inner and Outer Mongolia, to search travelers. Those from inland China going to Outer Mongolia are all arrested. (Twelfth Day Special Dispatch)

Peiping Business Community Resolves to Hold a Large Petition 26

Representatives from Various Counties and Cities in Hebei Province Issue Circular Telegram

(Peiping) This morning, the Peiping General Chamber of Commerce convened representatives from various gentry and merchant associations to a meeting, resolving to go to the Hebei Finance Special Commissioner's Office tomorrow morning to hold a large petition, demanding the fundamental abolition of the production and sales tax. Over a hundred representatives participated. (Twelfth Day Special Dispatch)

(Peiping) Representatives from various county and city chambers of commerce in Hebei province issued a circular telegram on the twelfth, detailing the reasons for requesting the abolition of the production and sales tax. It stated that the likin tax was transformed into a consumption tax, and then into a production and sales tax, which is eliminating one evil but creating a hundred others. Moreover, the production and sales tax lacks explicit written approval from the Ministry of Finance and has not been discussed and promulgated by the Legislative Yuan. Furthermore, it is not a uniformly applied tax law across the provinces. Such a production and sales tax, which hinders unification and violates laws and regulations, should be fundamentally abolished to save the thirty million merchants and people of Hebei from their suffering. (Twelfth Day Special Dispatch)

Representative Delegation of Refugees from Western Sichuan Sends Telegram

Li Zhuzhong's Troops Advance to Suppress Bandits in Wudang Mountain 34

The New Tenth Division Repels Red Bandits

Troops were dispatched to suppress them. On the sixth, they made contact with Guo Ziming's unit of the pseudo-Independent Seventh Division in Jiepai. The bandits were unable to withstand the attack and fled in disarray towards Chuanbu. Our army returned to Chongyang at noon on the eighth. Guo Rudong returned to Daye by boat on the twelfth, transferring to Yangxin. (Twelfth Day Special Dispatch)

(Hankou) Dai Minquan telegraphed Hankou on the twelfth, stating that his division was ordered to conduct a guerrilla campaign towards Yeji, successively defeating the Red Bandits in Caomiaoji, Hujiaji, Yejia Wafang, and Heiqiaowan. Currently, the main force of the bandits has fled to Lu'an, and a small force has fled to Shangcheng. (Twelfth Day Special Dispatch)

(Hankou) For the Peach Blossom Campaign of Xiao Zhichu's troops, in addition to issuing double pay to Xiao, Chiang also awarded 2,000 yuan, and Xu Yuanquan was awarded 500 yuan. (Twelfth Day Special Dispatch)

(Hankou) Chen Cheng sent Wu Ziyi to set up an office of the Eighteenth Army in Hankou. Li Haijie is scheduled to arrive in Hankou on the thirteenth. (Twelfth Day Special Dispatch)

(Hankou) The Military Headquarters appointed Cheng Ruhwai as a senior staff officer, and he assumed office on the twelfth. (Twelfth Day Special Dispatch)

Southern Shanxi Cannot Bear the Supply Burden 35

(Taiyuan) Although the Provincial Government has ordered the cessation of supplies to the stationed troops in various counties from June 1st, the stationed troops, on the grounds of purchasing shoes and socks, are still ordering the continuation of half of the burden. The military grain office has already been abolished, and military pay has not yet been issued. Local bandits are rising up everywhere, the wheat harvest is only 10-20%, the order of things is chaotic, and the people's food supply is cut off. Southern Shanxi has fallen into a state of extreme terror. (Twelfth Day Special Dispatch)

(Taiyuan) Jing Dingcheng, Xue Shixuan, Jing Yuzan, and other representatives from various counties in Hedong met with reporters from various newspapers in the Education Hall on the twelfth, reporting on the various tragic situations of the people's livelihood in southern Shanxi being devastated and bandits causing disturbances. They plan to unite all sectors of society to carry out a large-scale rescue movement. The steps to be taken are: 1) Request the guest military generals to sympathize with the people and reduce the supply burden; 2) Request the Provincial Government to order the counties to assist in sharing the burden equally; 3) Organize people's self-defense organizations. It is also heard that the people of Wenxi Jinxian have telegraphed the Provincial Government, stating that if there is no solution, they will stop remitting various land taxes and provincial funds and implement self-rescue. (Twelfth Day Special Dispatch)

Guangdong Province Shortens Defensive Lines 36

(Hong Kong) Guangdong has switched to a defensive posture against the Northeast Jiangxi armies and shortened the defensive lines. The final defensive line is Xiaoping River Village, Longyandong, Shougouling, and Shipai, which are attached to the provincial capital. Trenches are being dug day and night with great effort. Our country's President Wang was elected as a regular judge with a term of nine years. The court session opens on June 15th every year. This year, the first court session was postponed to August due to some reason. Important Foreign Telegrams

The President and Vice President of the South Manchuria Railway Company Resign 76

Uchida and Eguchi to Succeed

Tokyo, 12th (Dentus News Agency) - President Senge of the South Manchuria Railway Company has been ill for a long time. When former Prime Minister Hamaguchi was attacked, he had already expressed his intention to resign. Because he disagreed with Vice President Ohira, he did not want to entrust everything to Ohira after his resignation. In addition, many issues such as the reorganization of the South Manchuria Railway Company and the Showa Steel Works have not been resolved, and he wanted to resign after they were resolved. Therefore, he has delayed until now. Now, with his illness still showing no signs of improvement, he and Vice President Ohira have submitted their resignations one after another.

Tokyo, 12th (Dentus News Agency) - It has been decided that former Vice President Uchida Kōsai and former Mitsubishi Director Eguchi Sadazane will succeed as President and Vice President of the South Manchuria Railway Company. The Japanese government has given this matter deep consideration because the South Manchuria Railway Company has important diplomatic relations and requires someone with diplomatic skills and who is not related to political parties, so as to avoid the pattern of progress being affected by the changes in the cabinet as in the past. Uchida possesses both of these qualifications.

Peru Declares National Martial Law 77

Revolutionary Party Uprising Unsuccessful

Twenty-Five People Arrested

Reuters, New York, 11th—The provisional government of Peru in South America has declared national martial law due to attempts at revolution endangering public order. An order issued by the government today stipulates that police may use firearms to disperse any demonstrations or gatherings of four or more people who do not heed verbal warnings. Anyone suspected of inciting rebellion or treason, once proven, will be sentenced to death. According to official sources, twenty-five people have already been arrested, reportedly planning to start an uprising today.

Liberal Party Does Not Cooperate With Labour Party to the End

Reuters, London, 11th—The Liberal Party has scheduled a land tax amendment to be proposed in the House of Commons next week. This matter is not only important but also pressing. It is widely believed that the amendment is fully supported by the Conservative Party. Liberal leader George stated that the Liberal Party must present this case, not to make things difficult for the government, but to demand appropriate treatment for landowners.

Therefore, additional funds must be raised before July.

Summary of Important News 79

Collecting Taxes, The Reason Being That the Sino-Russian Conference Has Not Yet Decided on a Treaty. Once Taxes Are Collected (Russia Can Use It as an Excuse to Say That China Has Recognized Its Resumption of Trade, and Can Then Transport Goods to China in Large Quantities.) Currently, Several Train Cars Are Loaded Every Week and Distributed to Various Stations, Large and Small, Where They Are Sold Directly on the Trains. When Asked, They Claim to Be a Mobile Consumer Cooperative. However, the Purpose of the Eastern Railway Consumer Cooperative Is That, Except for Daily Necessities, They Are Not Allowed to Sell Other Items, and Are Not Allowed to Sell to Non-Railway Employees. Now, No Questions Are Asked, and Fearing That Non-Railway Employees Will Not Buy, Personnel Are Sent to Advertise Everywhere When Goods Arrive at Each Station, Soliciting Chinese and Foreign People to Board the Train and Purchase. Because the Goods Are Not Taxed and Do Not Bear Eastern Railway Shipping Costs, They Are Sold at Low Prices, and Sales Are Very Brisk. Every Week, At Least Every Small Station Can Sell One Train Car, and Large Stations Two or Three Train Cars. As a Result, Local Stores Are Greatly Affected. The Harbin Consumer Cooperative is also particularly active. Therefore, All Major Department Stores, Such as Tong Fa Long, Gong He Li, Fu He Chang, and Heng Shun Chang, Are Affected. In Order to Prevent Future Harm, the Merchants Recently Appealed to the General Chamber of Commerce, Requesting That It Be Forwarded to the Government to Prohibit Russian Merchants from Engaging in Activities Under False Names. In addition, the Special Zone Businessmen's Association Also Held a General Meeting A Few Days Ago, Resolving to Petition the Government Against the Revival of the Eastern Railway Consumer Cooperative. The Authorities Have Already Sent a Letter to Diplomatic Commissioner Zhong Yu, Asking Him to Negotiate With the Russian Consul in Harbin. It Is Also Heard That the Soviet Russian Government Stipulates That All Red Railway Employees Serving the Eastern Railway Must Use One-Quarter of Their Salary Each Month for Living Expenses, One-Quarter for Party Dues, and the Remaining Two-Quarters to Expand the Funding of the Mobile Consumer Cooperative, With More Than 1.7 Million Available Each Month, So Their Strength Is Quite Strong. (7th)

Tobacco Seedlings Everywhere in Suxian County 80

Numerous Soil Trading Firms in Various Townships

The Government Actually Collects Taxes for Protection

Xuzhou Correspondent, Southern Xuzhou is Adjacent to Northern Anhui. Suxian, Haoling, and Wo Counties in Anhui Province have always been famous for producing tobacco. Now is the time when tobacco seedlings are harvested in large quantities, and many people go to Suxian County to buy fresh soil. According to investigations, there are numerous soil trading firms in Suxian County, mostly in important townships, openly collecting taxes. The method of tax payment is annual, ranging from ten to twenty yuan per plot. The tax money is collected by the district chiefs of each district and turned over to the authorities. Soil trading firms collect three percent from both buyers and sellers of raw tobacco, making huge profits, and they are protected by the government. Approximately, there are fifteen soil trading firms in Xiezhuang, eight in Luji, eight in Baichu, six in Langanshan, twenty in Minxian Village, five in Jiagouzhi, thirty in Shicun, fifteen in Wangji, ten in Yinji, sixteen in Kantun, twenty-five in Lutun, nine in Zhichengzi, fifteen in Daozhuang, and eighteen in Xiaqiao. Other less important villages and towns also have three to several firms each. This is truly shocking. As for the places where tobacco is grown, they are everywhere you look. Ordinary residents with fifty mu of land will use twenty mu to grow tobacco. This is because each mu of good land can yield 140 to 150 taels of tobacco, while each mu of poor land can yield 50 to 60 taels of tobacco. The minimum price of tobacco is about one yuan per tael. And growing one hundred mu of tobacco can be reported as forty or fifty mu. The tax on each mu of tobacco seedlings is set at fifty yuan. Based on profit calculations, many people are happy to grow it. However, this year, the official tobacco seedling tax is set at one hundred yuan per mu, and most growers oppose it. Currently, the district and township chiefs are petitioning the province for instructions on how to proceed. It is said that the tobacco growing situation in various counties in northern Anhui is roughly the same as in Suxian County. (10th)

Fine Qin and Han Bricks and Tiles Have Been Seized by the Japanese 81

The Entire Collection of Bricks and Tiles is Worth Only 2,500 Yuan

Jinan Correspondent, After the entire collection of Qin and Han bricks and tiles, the only national treasure collected by the Gao family of Weixian County, was bought by the Japanese, it was detained by the Jiaoji Railway Bureau when passing through Qingdao. The railway bureau and the Qingdao municipal government jointly sealed the antiques and sent police to guard them day and night to prevent accidents. However, although the Law on the Preservation of Antiques has been drafted by the central government, it has not yet been officially promulgated and implemented. Therefore, the Department of Education telegraphed the Ministry of Education for instructions, and the Jiaoji Railway Bureau also requested instructions from the Ministry of Railways, and forwarded them to the Ministry of Education and the Executive Yuan for handling. However, according to recent confirmed investigations, the essence of the Qin and Han bricks and tiles has been seized by the Japanese. According to a gentleman in Qingdao who learned from the Japanese, this collection of bricks and tiles was purchased by Ota, a famous Japanese antique dealer. Kuhara, who is currently in charge of negotiations, is a transportation agent and also a small Japanese antique dealer. After Ota bought it, he took the best two Qin bricks back to his country. These two are Qin twelve-character bricks, which are the best of the Qin and Han bricks and tiles. The Shandong Provincial Library once had a rubbing of this brick. According to the hall style, the brick is inscribed with twelve characters: "All within the seas are subjects, the years bring abundant harvests, and there are no hungry people." The brick is square, approximately eight inches in length, width, and height. The brick is stored in a wooden box, with the words written by Wang Yirong. The original text reads: "The twelve characters are all from the words of Zhuan Hansheng, designated as Qin leg, Mr. Weng Ge said that the era is determined by the characters. I am planning to use this sentence to congratulate the present family of heaven, Yi Rong Ji." According to the text, "Jun" is a Ding rhyme character, "Zhuan" is an ancient brick character, and Hansheng is the son of Gao Qingling. This box was made by Gao Hansheng, and Gao Hansheng also wrote a poem himself and attached it to it. The value of its nobleness can be imagined. The one currently detained in Qingdao is still a twelve-character brick, which is also a supreme treasure. The total price of all the bricks and tiles is 2,500 yuan. Gong, the negotiator, received 900 yuan, and the Gao family received no more than 1,600 yuan. It is regrettable to sell the only national treasure for this meager amount of money. (10th)

Local Correspondences

Songjiang 82

All District Chiefs Telegraph to Retain County Chief The Songjiang County Chief, Jin Qingzhang, has been in office for three years. Today, news was received from the province that Shen Yong was transferred to Changsong. Upon hearing the news, all the district chiefs sent a telegram to the Civil Affairs Department of the Provincial Government to request his retention. The telegram roughly stated: "Songjiang County Chief Jin Qingzhang has served for three years and has an outstanding reputation. The people of Songjiang are celebrating the acquisition of talent, hoping that he will display his talents to complete the construction of New Songjiang. Upon hearing of the transfer, the whole county was shocked. We hereby telegraph our plea, earnestly requesting that Your Excellency heed public opinion and quickly withdraw the order, so as to comfort the expectations of the people."

Qingpu 83

Family Dispute Leads to Murder Chen Ahe of Dujia Village, Tenth District, because his younger brother A Lin married three wives, which depleted a lot of property, had a big dispute with his father. A few days ago, Ahe angrily wanted to kill his wife and remarry. His uncle heard about it and went to mediate. Ahe not only did not listen but turned to his uncle with an evil attitude, causing the uncle to strike him twice. Afterwards, Ahe suddenly became abnormal and wanted to die. The family was terrified. As a result, Ahe secretly hanged himself in his uncle's shed. By the time it was discovered, he had already stopped breathing.

Fengxian 84

The Groom Falls to the Ground at the Wedding Sedan The groom, Sheng Youzi of Sheng Zaimao Flower Village, Shitou River, North of Shengzi Temple, married Zhang, a woman from Xitan, Songjiang, for his son Buchan yesterday. Sheng has always been stubborn, so all the wedding ceremonies were in accordance with customs. In addition to setting up an incense table in the hall to pay homage to heaven and earth, before the wedding sedan arrived at the door, he ordered the groom to go outside the city to greet it, emphasizing the importance of the ceremony. Unexpectedly, upon returning to the hall, the groom suddenly vomited blood and fell unconscious. Immediately, the whole family was in panic and at a loss. Superstitious people said that he had offended the flower powder deity and asked for prayers. The Sheng family also believed that the time was conflicting and beat the astrologer who had chosen the day, causing his head to bleed and almost causing a major disaster. Fortunately, his relative Huang hired Dr. Xu Tianxiang to give acupuncture treatment and wake him up. However, Sheng believed that the auspicious time had passed and the wedding was not completed, so he specially rescheduled the wedding for today to show perfection.

Suzhou 85

Business Tax to Be Levied Soon The Wu County business tax has not been levied because the recognized amount does not match the budget of the province. Yesterday (12th) morning, Song Youpei, a representative of the money industry, Wang Hongbin, a representative of the gold and silver industry, and Jin Yian, a representative of the tea, food, and candy industry, all went to the business tax bureau to discuss practical solutions with Director Wang. It is said that other industries are also going to make contact. The date of the levy is likely to be far off.

The Bandit Suppression Headquarters is Ready The governments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces have decided to set up a Taihu Bandit Suppression Headquarters in Suzhou. The commander, Zhu Mian, has sent personnel to Suzhou to survey the location.

Zhang Liyun's Divorce Appeal Rejected Zhang Liyun, a wealthy household in Hengjing who moved to Darning Alley in Suzhou City, had disagreements with his wife Xu Shouzhen and filed a divorce lawsuit with the local court. The lawsuit was rejected after the trial. Zhang was not satisfied with the judgment and appealed to the High Court. Yesterday (12th), the High Court ruled that the appeal was rejected, and the litigation costs were to be borne by the appellant.

Zhuang Yanyan Does Not Hand Over the Account Zhuang Yan, the former county chief of Nantong County, had unclear handover procedures when he left office and lived in Suzhou City to avoid accountability. The province has repeatedly ordered him to go to Nantong to liquidate the accounts as soon as possible, but Zhuang ignored it and delayed it for a long time without resolving it. Yesterday (12th), County Chief Huang of Wu County received another telegram from the Finance Department ordering him to send someone to escort Zhuang to Nantong to handle the handover.

Wuxi 86

Wanshi City Reported Another Robbery The sixteenth district (Wanshi City), residents of Qudong Village, Xian Genquan's family, at about 10 o'clock on the night of the 11th, suddenly had more than 20 bandits, wrapped in white cloth, armed with guns, iron rulers, wooden sticks, flashlights, and other weapons, breaking into the house, looting and searching, and leaving with stolen goods after about an hour. After inspection, it was counted that dozens of yuan in cash and gold and silver jewelry, clothing, and other items were stolen, with a total loss of more than 200 yuan.

Party and Government Agencies Mediate Fire Disputes In Ni Chunji's carpentry shop behind Chen Baitou Alley on Tonghui Road in this city, a fire broke out suddenly and unexpectedly at 10:30 on the evening of the 11th, causing a conflagration. In an instant, the fire was blazing, and it was impossible to approach it. Nearby residents rang gongs to warn the police. After hearing the police, the Zhoushanbang Fire Brigade of this area immediately drove the dragon to the scene and tried their best to put out the fire, but the fire was too fierce and the effort was of little help. Because the other fire brigades inside and outside the city had opinions with the Zhongnan Grand Theater, the captains of each team published a joint announcement in the local newspaper, unanimously resigning from their respective associations. As there has not yet been a proper solution, all the fire brigades did not drag the dragon out to put out the fire, which caused the fire to spread, burning for two hours. Seventy or eighty thatched huts were burned to ashes, with a loss of about 4,500 yuan. When the fire was raging, the crying of the distressed thatched households was deafening, and the situation was very pitiful. Unexpectedly, at about 10 o'clock yesterday morning, a fire broke out suddenly in the Hou family's firewood room on Yingshan River in the city. For a time, gongs rang in the streets and alleys, but no water dragon went to put out the fire, allowing the god of fire to show its power. Soon, the Hou family's firewood room was turned into scorched earth. County Chief Pan Zhongjia and the county party rectification committee Zhang Hantian and Hu Nianqian, etc., because of the continuous fires in recent days and no one to rescue them, convened a meeting of various agencies and groups in the county government at 2 o'clock in the afternoon to discuss rescue measures.

Changzhou 87

A Robbery Occurred Outside the City The Xiaowangjia Village, about two miles outside the Danan Gate of Wuyi, has only four families: Wang Yinda, Wang Shengda, Wang Zhaoda, and Bi Liansheng. At about 10 o'clock on the evening of the 10th, more than a dozen armed bandits suddenly arrived at the village to rob. None of the four families were spared. Because there was not much cash, Wang Yinda was hung up and beaten, and foreign candles were burned under his ribs, causing serious injuries. The bandits searched until dawn on the 11th before leaving with the stolen goods.

The Department Commission Investigates Menghu The excavation of Menghu in Wuyi is about to be completed. The Construction Bureau previously submitted a request to the Construction Department to send someone to Changzhou for inspection. The department has commissioned Zhang Shuyuan to come to Changzhou on the 11th. On the 12th, he went to the countryside with Zhuang Zhongxi, the director of the Construction Bureau, for investigation.

Danyang 88

Police Beaten for Arresting Gamblers When the Fourth Public Security Branch of Fangxianqiao heard that gambling was often taking place in the teahouse opened by Sun Yang in Yangshu Village, they sent a senior police officer to arrest the gamblers. Four gamblers were captured on the spot. Then, Xu Qifeng, the deputy village chief, heard the news and went to mediate. At this time, there were many onlookers. Suddenly, a misunderstanding occurred, resulting in a beating. As a result, two senior police officers were injured and reported back to the bureau. Cao, the chief of the branch bureau, was furious and personally led the police to the village and arrested seven people, including the village deputy Xu Qifeng and the teahouse owner Sun Yang. They have now been sent to the county bureau for investigation.

Leaping From a Train and Crushed to Death A man named Xu from Zaze, Zhenyi, came to Danyang on a Xining commuter train the other night and missed his stop without realizing it. When the train arrived at Xiaomaoshan, Xu panicked and jumped out of the train window, falling into the track. The wheels ran over him, his head and body separated, and he died tragically.

Zhenjiang 89

Change of Fifth District Chief Jiang Chaoxiong, the chief of the Fifth District of Waterborne Public Security, was transferred to the chief of the Fourth District of Water Police after a decision by the provincial government. The vacant position will be concurrently held by Cheng Zhuang, the chief of the Sixth District. Jiang is currently rushing to handle the handover. Zhang Hengyao Committed Two Crimes Zhang Hengyao, a resident of Dashu Town, was charged with instigating remarriage and was accused by the Zhenjiang Local Court. He was also accused of fraud by the Shanghai Special Zone Court. Both cases were found to be true after investigation and were sentenced to three years and six months of imprisonment. He was transferred back to Zhenjiang yesterday to be executed in the original county.

Jurong 90

Daughter-in-Law Commits Suicide by Swallowing Opium Due to Abuse by Mother-in-Law Gao, the wife of Li in Sunjiabian Village, Taiping Township, Fifth District, was violent and fierce. Her husband could do nothing about it, and her son was often humiliated and scolded. Gao, who was pure and kind, was disliked by her son and her daughter-in-law. Gao abused and abused her and scolded her at every turn, Zhao could not bear the abuse, and committed suicide by swallowing opium a few days ago.

Yangzhou 91

Commander Liang's Bandit Suppression Plan The Pacification Supervisor Zhang Zhijiang, according to Commander Liang Guanying's telegram, stated that the two gangs of bandits, Wei Yousan and Liu Rongfeng, totaling more than 800 people with 500 or 600 guns, have occupied more than 20 villages in the Da Gu Village, Sunjiaqiao, Tao Yuemiao, and Baowei areas, burning, killing, and looting, which is extremely rampant. He has ordered Liu Brigade to arrive at the Shajiwei, Shangqinwei, Taozhuang, Houlou, Wangwei, Hanzhuang, and Sanjietang line by 2:00 am of the following day, and to deploy strictly to begin attacking the villages occupied by the bandits at 3:00 am on the same day. He requested that the 3rd Cavalry Division be dispatched to the Xiawei east of Gaozuo by 2:00 am of the following day, and to immediately occupy the Xiawei Fulin Qiu Ji Zang Jaba line, and to set up a tight defense to cooperate in the attack. He also requested that the Anhui Army Xutuan stationed in Si be instructed to arrive at the northern end of Xiaodeng Xiaoliu Chishan by 2:00 am on the same day, to set up a tight blockade and to take contact with Liu Brigade at any time, in order to annihilate them in one fell swoop. Yesterday (10th), in addition to sending a telegram to the 3rd Cavalry Division, he also sent a telegram to Chairman Chen of Anhui, instructing Xutuan stationed in Si to follow Commander Liang's original plan for coordinated suppression.

Causes and Consequences of Huaiyin's Pig Tax Dispute 92

Huaiyin's pig tax and police donations are due to competition, and a small number of pig merchants went to the province to petition for cancellation. The Civil Affairs Department once rejected the request, and involved the Public Security Bureau in detaining ships and escorting people. The County Government reported the facts to the Civil Affairs Department, stating that the pig tax collection was in accordance with the Department's orders and approved the original plan for implementation, and that the county had instructed the collection of donations and that the detention of ships was not true. As for the case of Chen Ruyi assaulting the police, it was another matter and has been handled according to judicial procedures. The Civil Affairs Department replied and ordered the merchants to quickly return to the county to discuss the payment methods, stating that the merchant donations and public security funds should be taken into account, and there was no need to bother the province any further. Ye Daxing and other pig farms have agreed to the original amount with the County Government and will continue to pay monthly to resolve the dispute.

Qingjiang 93

A Bizarre Murder Occurred Outside the City In the Taiping Gang Alley in Hebei, outside Huaiyin City, the Lu Kai Rong family rented a house to Wu Yin Hou, a resident of Daxing Village in this county, through the introduction of Jiang Fengke. Yin Hou returned to Daxing Village on the 3rd of this month to harvest wheat, leaving his wife Shi in the residence. On the evening of the 7th, two farmers known to Shi went to stay overnight, claiming that they had come from the countryside to Pu to sell pigs and had not had time to return. Gu, Kai Rong's mother, did not want to let them stay overnight because the two people were of unknown origin. Shi said that they were acquaintances, so Gu was reluctant to refuse. Unexpectedly, at about 1:00 AM, Gu heard Wu's children crying non-stop. When she went to check, she saw that the people who had stayed overnight had left, and Wu's wife Shi's face was covered in blood. Only then did she realize that she had been killed. She immediately woke up her son Kai Rong and reported it to the Public Security Bureau. The bureau dispatched a patrol officer to investigate and placed the Lu mother and son under surveillance. Another guard, Zhang Yu, was called to guard the body. On the 8th, they went to the county to report and asked for an examination. As for Wu Yin Hou, he had not returned to the residence by the afternoon of the 8th. It is unknown how this bizarre murder will end.

Taixian County 94

The New Achievements of the Chief of the Public Security Bureau Since taking office, Shen Yi, the Chief of the Public Security Bureau of this county, has been determined to reform and strictly reorganized the staff and police officers. On the 10th of this month, he held a county-wide police affairs meeting to consider the situation in various places, standardize police expenses, and carry out the work with all his strength. He paid particular attention to the three items of opium, gambling, and prostitution, but because of the long-standing customs in Taixian County, it was difficult to change, so he started with persuasion to promote self-repentance. If persuasion was ineffective, he would impose severe punishments to enforce the law and promote self-renewal. Other aspects, such as preparing training grounds, organizing cleanliness and hygiene, and setting up patrol boxes, are also being actively carried out.
