Huzhou 96

A Boat Robbed Midway A boat from Canhuan Field outside the North Gate of this city, carrying eight silk-selling villagers, returned to the village from the city at about 4:00 PM on the 8th of this month. While passing through the Chang'an Port area, a bandit boat suddenly appeared with three bandits. Two bandits pulled out handguns and ordered them to stop. The passengers were afraid to resist and had to let the bandits search. Except for passenger Shen, who took the opportunity to enter the river and swim away, the other seven were not spared. The money from the silk sales was all robbed, with a total loss of more than 800 yuan. Afterwards, boat owner Pan Hubao went to Daqian to report the robbery to the 14th Water Police Team. After receiving the report, the team immediately sent a team to investigate. At about 2:00 PM on the 9th, the 1st Water Police Team arrested the three bandits involved in the case, Jiao Ganchen, Xu Atian, and Peng Chen, and took them back for interrogation.

Xiaoshan 97

Dispute Over a Boat Landing Leads to Murder Farmers Cao and Tang in Aozaochen, south of Xiaoshan Gate, quarreled over a river mud boat landing, and then the two sides beat each other. A worker surnamed Cao was beaten in the chest by Tang, fainted and fell to the ground, and died on the night of the 11th. Tang, because he caused the murder, first went to the county court to examine the wounds. Today, Cao also reported the murder and requested an examination.

Night Sailboat Encountered Robbery On the night of the 11th, at about 9:00 PM, a sailboat full of groceries, etc., sailing from Shaoxing to Linpu, was stopped by a bandit boat. There were a total of seven or eight bandits. They robbed all the silk and silk threads, etc., worth 500 yuan, and also robbed three foreign letters, with a total of 150 yuan in cash.

Wuhu 98

Merchant Ship Robbed in Chaohu Wuhu Correspondent, The incidents of passenger ships traveling on the Yangtze River and other inland rivers in Anhui Province being robbed midway and goods being stolen have been frequently reported in recent years. Although the authorities have repeatedly ordered strict investigations, the banditry has not diminished. On the 9th of this month, the Sheng An small wheel, which runs from Wuhu to Sanhe, Hefei, was robbed at Chaohu Estuary. The wheel sailed from Wuhu to Sanhe, and at about 2:00 PM it entered the Chaohu Estuary, and suddenly four thugs shouted and rose up from among the passengers, each holding a box gun and firing into the air. They immediately crowded into the rudder room, forced the captain to stop the wheel, and after a while, a bandit boat drove swiftly from the north bank, and seven bandits also fired their guns in response, jumped on the wheel, first went to the accounting room, forcing them to reveal the place where the money was hidden, and after the crew stated that they had not shipped a large amount of money, the bandits dispersed to search, and all the passengers' money and goods were looted, and after an hour, they left in the original boat. The total loss was about 4,000 yuan, with a certain cocoon merchant suffering the most. After the bandits left, the wheel continued to sail towards Sanhe, and today it returned to Wuhu, and has reported the robbery to the Shipping Association, which has forwarded it to the military and police agencies, requesting a strict investigation.

Letter to the Editor

Letter from the Telecommunications Department of the Ministry of Communications 99

Dear Editor, I recently read in your newspaper on June 5th that representatives of the Great Eastern, Great Northern, and Pacific Underwater Cable Companies met with Zhong Er, Director of the Telecommunications Department of the Ministry of Communications, etc., on the afternoon of the 4th, and further studied the landing and other matters in the previously drafted underwater cable contract. After investigation, the meeting between the Ministry and representatives of the three underwater cable companies on June 4th was about the issue of overdue underwater cable fees from various telegraph offices. The previous report was inconsistent with the facts. I am sending this letter to request that you investigate and make corrections. Sincerely, The Telecommunications Department of the Ministry of Communications.

Vow to Reject Wu Nanxuan's Return to School

| Professor and Student Representatives Go to Beijing |

Beijing, 12th – Tsinghua University students held a general assembly this morning and resolved to vow to reject Wu Nanxuan's return to school, organize an armed school protection group, and send a telegram to the Ministry of Education stating that the original professors, not having received next term's contracts, will all leave the school to take other positions. They requested the Ministry find a way to renew their contracts.

Beijing Central News – Tsinghua University students resolved to organize an armed school protection group to vow to reject Wu Nanxuan's return to school. On the 11th, they telegraphed the Ministry of Education requesting the continued employment of next semester's professors to emphasize academics, and dispatched three representatives to Beijing to petition. Furthermore, the Professors' Association also nominated Feng Youlan, Zhang Xiruo, and Wu Zhengzhi as three representatives, scheduled to go south today or tomorrow, requesting the Ministry of Education resolve the Tsinghua student unrest as soon as possible.

(Beijing Correspondence) – Since the outbreak of the school president turmoil at Tsinghua University, the Ministry of Education telegraphed the president of Peking University, Jiang Menglin, requesting him to investigate the matter nearby. Mr. Jiang personally went to Tsinghua University a few days ago, announced the Ministry of Education's handling methods, and promised to take full responsibility for mediation. According to a certain source, Mr. Jiang has been working hard on this matter for several days. It is also heard that Mr. Jiang has telegraphed the Ministry, suggesting recommending Feng Youlan as acting president.

The graduating class of Tsinghua University's fourth year students sent representatives yesterday to visit President Wu Nanxuan to discuss the graduation trip fee issue. The usual travel fee for Tsinghua is eighty yuan. The students now hope to increase it to one hundred and fifty yuan, it is said.

According to Wu Nanxuan's statement to people yesterday (the 8th), before the Ministry of Education approves his resignation request, he will be absolutely responsible for Tsinghua's school affairs, but he is determined not to cling to his position and has sent a sincere telegram to the Ministry of Education.

Zhejiang Province Education Turmoil Unresolved 101

Provincial Government Again Persuades Zhang Daofan to Stay

Chairman Zhang Goes to Beijing to Urge Retention

Zhejiang Education Director Zhang Daofan submitted his resignation, which was retained by order of the Provincial Government and the Ministry of Education. Provincial Middle School Education Association Representative Conference 102

Requests Government to Issue Education Funds on Schedule

Disdainful of Warning from Education Department's Shen Lu

Requests Ministry of Education to Appoint Education Director Quickly

The Zhejiang Provincial Middle School Teachers' Association believes that individual school strikes are too sacrificial, and the teachers' meetings of various schools have repeatedly sent letters requesting a representative conference to be convened to jointly resolve the issue. Therefore, the Standing Committee notified the schools to postpone individual actions and scheduled a representative conference to be held on the 10th of this month at the Hangzhou Provincial Senior High School. It is now learned that the conference was held yesterday (the 10th). Attendees included high school teacher representatives Shi Bohou and Hong Zhituo, First Middle School representatives Zhu Husheng and Wei Fuxiang, Second Middle School representative Cai Yanyou, Third Middle School representative Shen Jia, Fourth Middle School representatives Zhang Zhuzhong and Wu Yuefang, Fifth Middle School representatives Jin Zhiwen and Chen Yude, Sixth Middle School representative Cai Yuze, Seventh Middle School representatives Jiang Chengbiāo and Luo Songtao, Eighth Middle School representative Xu Baoyan, Ninth Middle School representative Sun Baigang, Tenth Middle School representative Li Jizhang, Sericulture Middle School representatives Zheng Zhenxia, Zhou Tianyu, and Miao Dehai, among more than twenty others. The main cases resolved in the two meetings on the 10th and 11th are recorded below: 1. Regarding the case of whether to approve the request of the Provincial Sericulture Middle School Teachers' Association to send representatives to join this association, it was resolved to allow them to join this association. 2. Regarding the case of how to urge the allocation of education funds for provincial schools this semester, it was resolved to request the government to issue the funds for March and April before June 20, and to issue the funds for May before the end of this semester's vacation. The funds for June and July must also be allocated on schedule. If the funds for March and April are not issued before June 20, and the funds for May are not issued before the end of the vacation, then all schools will not conduct exams, handle closing procedures, or submit exhibits to the Provincial Middle School Achievement Exhibition after the 20th. Furthermore, the funds for middle schools outside the provincial capital, such as the Third, Fourth, Sixth, Seventh, Eighth, Ninth, Tenth, and Eleventh Middle Schools, must be directly disbursed by the provincial treasury, and a letter should be sent to the principals of the provincial middle schools requesting them to inform the government. Meanwhile, representatives should be sent to present the matter to the provincial government. 3. Regarding the case of whether to raise questions about the Education Department Secretary Shen Lu's absurd language when meeting with representatives of various school teachers previously, it was resolved to disdain questioning him. 4. Regarding the case of sending telegrams to the Ministry of Education and the Provincial Government requesting them to forward to the National Government the request for the current Director Zhang to resign and to quickly appoint a capable successor, it was resolved to send telegrams. 5. Regarding the resolution of the Nanjing June 6th Teachers' Day celebration conference to designate June 6th as Teachers' Day and organize a National Teachers' Association, it was resolved to approve the resolution. 6. It was resolved to pass the resolution on publishing the association's declaration. It is also heard that the association has many other proposals and is scheduled to continue the meeting on the 12th.

Jiangsu Education Department Orders Issuance of Revised Regulations on the Appointment, Dismissal, and Treatment of Provincial and County Elementary School Principals 103

The Jiangsu Provincial Education Department issued instructions to the education bureaus of various counties, stating that the department, because of the Jiangsu Provincial and County Elementary School Principals Appointment, Dismissal, and Treatment Provisional Regulations' provisions regarding the qualifications of elementary school principals, had difficulties in implementation. It had revised the provisions of item A in Article 3 of the original regulations according to the actual situation and submitted them to the Jiangsu Provincial Government for approval and implementation. Now, it has received instructions, which state, "The submission is noted. The case has been approved at the 403rd meeting of the government committee. In addition to informing the Ministry for record, you are to be informed. This order." Therefore, the revised provisions of item A in Article 3 are copied and issued, ordering the bureau directors to comply with this order.

The revised provisions of item A in Article 3 of the Provisional Regulations on Appointment, Dismissal, and Treatment are as follows:

Article 3: The principals of various elementary schools shall be qualified if they have high moral character, adhere to party principles, and possess one of the following qualifications: (A) 1. Graduates of elementary schools, normal schools, or normal departments of senior high schools or above who have served as elementary school teachers for more than two years. 2. Graduates of specialized schools or above who have held primary education positions for more than two years and have achieved outstanding results. 3. Graduates of senior high schools or old-system middle schools who have thoroughly studied primary education and have served as elementary school head teachers for more than four years. 4. Graduates of rural normal schools, county normal schools, or normal training courses of three years or more who have served as elementary school head teachers for more than four years and have indeed conducted research with proven achievements.

The examination location will be Datong University, South Shanghai Railway Station. 4. Meals and accommodation during the examination period will be provided by the committee, which is currently in discussion with Datong University to handle the arrangements. Examination schedule: July 12, morning: Party Principles, Chinese, English; afternoon: physical examination. July 15, morning: mathematics; afternoon: oral examination. July 16, morning: chemistry, physics. 6. For those applying to universities in Jiangsu and Zhejiang that conduct early admissions, such as Jinling, Datong, and Soochow Universities, applicants to this committee may take those exams first.

Datong High School Establishes Civil Engineering Department 113

Datong High School on Jiaozhou Road in this city is a complete middle school attached to Datong University. The junior high school lasts three years, and the senior high school, starting from the first grade, is divided into three departments: general studies, teacher training, and commerce. To meet social needs and promote vocational education, it has been decided to add a senior high school civil engineering department starting next semester, with the aim of cultivating technical personnel such as drafters, supervisors, and surveyors. The curriculum and all equipment for the department are currently being planned and purchased. Only new students for the first grade are being recruited at present. All junior high school graduates may apply, it is said.

Guanghua University Affiliated Middle School Plans Summer School 114

Since Dr. Liao Maoru took over Guanghua University Affiliated Middle School, the school's reputation has grown daily, and its achievements have been remarkable, which has long been known to people at home and abroad. This semester, Dr. Liao resigned from his concurrent position as vice president of the university to focus on the progress of the affiliated middle school. The excellence of its achievements can be imagined. Recently, the school has also recognized that while many students can concentrate on self-study during the summer vacation, it is also unavoidable that some waste their time. Therefore, it has specially planned to run a summer school for Chinese, English, and mathematics this year. On the one hand, it will provide an opportunity for those with aspirations to pursue advanced studies, and on the other hand, it will enable those with weaker academic performance to engage in remedial work to make up for deficiencies, so that basic subjects can be fully developed. It is currently being planned, and it is heard that non-students of the school may also register for admission.

National Games Revises Sports Competition Rules 125

The National Games Preparatory Committee, in view of the imminent opening date,

The rules for various sports competitions should be actively compiled and printed. Most of these rules adopt those stipulated by the World Games and the Far Eastern Games, but there are also important changes. To make it clear to all places and to provide for the participation of those preparing, the following are selected and recorded:

Men's Hurdles 126

For the men's 400-meter hurdles, each lane should have ten hurdles. The height of the hurdles is 0.9145 meters. The distance from the starting line to the first hurdle is 45 meters. The distance between each hurdle is 35 meters. The distance from the tenth hurdle to the finish line is 40 meters.

Women's Track and Field 127

(A) For the 80-meter hurdles, each lane should have eight hurdles. The height of the hurdles is 0.762 meters (2.5 feet). The distance from the starting line to the first hurdle and from the eighth hurdle to the finish line is 13 meters. The distance between each hurdle is 8 meters. (B) Javelin. (1) (Construction) Made of wood with a tip made of iron or copper. The distance from the point to the tip of the javelin should not exceed 0.95 meters or be shorter than 0.80 meters. (2) (Handle) Wrapped with a 16-meter-wide string at the center of gravity as a handle. The string must be smooth and free of knots. The diameter of both ends must not be more than 25 millimeters larger than the javelin rod. There must be no other similar objects on the javelin rod other than the string of the handle. (3) (Length) The whole body must be at least 2.20 meters long. (4) (Weight) Must not be lighter than 600 grams.

Men's Basketball 128

In the center circle jump ball, dribbling is not allowed before the ball reaches its highest point, and leaving the center circle is not allowed before the ball is dribbled. A maximum of two dribbles are allowed. The center is not allowed to touch the ball again without any of the other eight people touching or touching the ground, or the basket, or the backboard. Also, if an opponent violates the personal foul rule while a player is throwing the ball into the basket, if the ball fails to be thrown in as a result, two free throws should be awarded. If the ball is still thrown in and is valid, then only one free throw is awarded. As for women's basketball, the dual-zone system is still used.

Men's Volleyball 129

(Serving) Players are allowed one error for each serve. If there are two consecutive errors, it is a failure, and their opponent gets one point.

Men's and Women's Tennis 130

The Davis Cup method is adopted. Each team has a maximum of four people. Each match between two teams has a total of four singles matches and one doubles match. First, Team A's first singles plays against Team B's first singles, and Team A's second singles plays against Team B's second singles. Then, the doubles match is played. After that, Team A's first singles plays against Team B's second singles, and Team B's first singles plays against Team A's second singles. The singles matches before and after must be the original players. However, both sides can freely substitute their other two players.

All Sectors Unanimously Support the Shutdown of the National Products Market 140

The China National Products United Department Store was ordered to close by the工部局(The Shanghai Municipal Council). The situation has now expanded. Yesterday, both the Taxpayers' Association and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent letters to the工部局(The Shanghai Municipal Council) to question them. The negotiation committee and support association organized by the department store have also been formally established, and the industrial, commercial, and academic circles are unanimously providing assistance. The External Affairs Office and the National Goods Exhibition Hall have all sent personnel to investigate the truth. The situation yesterday is recorded separately below:

Party Headquarters News 141

(1) The Municipal Executive Committee's Attention: The Municipal Party Headquarters regards promoting national goods as one of the party's seven movements, and national goods are a powerful weapon to block the annual outflow of 120 million. Today, the imperialists are deeply afraid that economic aggression will be severely hit, so they have taken preemptive measures, even ordering the police to seal it off, which is considered to be despising Chinese merchants and infringing on national rights. Therefore, it was brought up for discussion at the 115th Standing Committee meeting yesterday. It was resolved to send a letter to the Municipal Government to seriously negotiate with the authorities of the Public Concession. (2) Declaration of the Third District Party Headquarters: The Third District Party Headquarters issued a declaration yesterday, which said: (The above omitted. This city's China National Products Department Store is the hub for promoting national goods. Recently, it has been envied by the British police, who have used false pretexts and illegal means to close it down and beat up employees. Upon hearing this, we are deeply indignant. The imperialists rely on the development of science and the progress of machinery to use surplus goods as the only strategy for economic aggression against China. The establishment of the National Products Department Store fundamentally conflicts with this kind of aggression. The police under the rule of the British imperialists do not hesitate to use the licensing issue of the amusement part of the department store as a pretext to illegally close it down. The place has been a New World amusement park for many years, and the relocation of the National Products Department Store has not even been a旬(ten days). If it is said that the equipment is not complete or the building is not solid, and it is closed down, then why was a license issued when the New World amusement park was opened, and why was it closed down only on the day the National Products Department Store opened? Moreover, the department store is located downstairs, while the amusement part is upstairs. If it is believed that the amusement part has not been licensed, so it is closed down as a reason, then it is only necessary to stop or close down the amusement part. Why must the department store part be involved? After repeated consideration, it is impossible not to think that there is another intention. Moreover, the insults to employees and the arbitrary arrests fully reveal the hideous faces of the imperialists. However, within our national territory, allowing them to be so barbaric is simply unthinkable. The occurrence of this incident happens to be seven days after the inauguration of the Chinese consultants and Chinese members of the Municipal Council in the Public Concession, which gives us a great lesson, making us realize that the piecemeal solution is not reliable, and the policy of bargaining with the imperialists is not advisable. We should follow the spirit of the General's fearlessness, follow the instructions of the National Assembly, and work together for the abolition of the treaties, so that the whole problem can be solved once and for all. In addition to leading all party members in the district to expand publicity, this association hereby declares, for your information.)

Attention from the Ministry of Industry 142

The Ministry of Industry believes that the Shanghai National Goods Department Store was founded by Zhang Zilian and others by raising shares and has been in business for more than a year. In the market in Shanghai where foreign goods are flooded, the department store only sells domestic products, which is closely related to the promotion of domestic products. Now, for what reason it was closed, the truth is unknown. In addition to telegraphing the Industrial and Commercial Visiting Bureau, the Shanghai Social Affairs Bureau, and the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, together with the Chinese Taxpayers Association and the Chinese directors, to find ways to help, it also believes that the 工部局(The Shanghai Municipal Council)'s closure of the Shanghai department store is related to diplomacy and has代(on behalf of) telegraphed the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, requesting that the ministry's Shanghai office be notified to investigate and handle it immediately.

Official Investigation 143

Since the Shanghai office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs sent representatives to the China National Goods Department Store the day before yesterday to request assistance, in addition to reporting to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for consideration and requesting instructions, yesterday, Director Yang also sent staff member Tang Ruxuan to investigate both sides based on reports from various parties to determine the truth, so that it could be submitted to the ministry for reference. In addition, Dong Keren, curator of the National Goods Exhibition Hall in this city, believes that this matter is closely related to the future of domestic products. Yesterday, he also personally went to various parties to investigate the truth so that he could report it to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau and propose serious negotiations.

Reception for the Press 144

The negotiation committee of the National Products Department Store has been formally established, and Zhang Zilian and ten others have been appointed as members. Yesterday afternoon at 3 o'clock, the committee held a tea party for newspaper reporters at the Atlantic Restaurant on Fourth Road. More than 50 reporters from various newspapers attended. Chairman Zhang Zilian and member Chen Weixin reported on the progress, followed by a speech by Xie Fusheng, which ended at 6 o'clock.

Letter from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce 145

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Council yesterday, which read: "Dear Sirs, on the 11th of this month, we received a letter from the China National Products United Department Store stating that they founded the China National Products United Department Store on Nanjing Road in Shanghai in July of last year. In May of this year, they moved the department store to the west side of Jing'an Temple Road and continued to operate as usual. Unexpectedly, at 3 p.m. on June 9, the Public Concession police suddenly sent police officers to order the business to stop, locking all the doors of the entire venue and sending police to monitor and prevent entry and exit. Zhang Zian and Liu Musu, employees of the three-week cotton weaving factory, were beaten up by the doormen when they came to the venue for business. Department store employees Wang Jianxin and Hua Zusheng were arrested and detained in the police station when they went out. Even the people who brought meals were prevented from bringing rice into the venue. Our chamber of commerce was unable to resist under the pressure of force and had to suspend business. We are now sending a letter to inform you of the process and ask for your assistance. The department store is renting the old site of the New World. After renting the site, the department store has used part of the hall as a department store and the rest as an amusement area, with separate managers responsible for each. According to your bureau's regulations, amusement parks must have a license, while department stores do not need to obtain a license. This time, because the equipment and facilities of the amusement department did not meet the instructions of your bureau, the so-called suspension of business should also be limited to the amusement department. The department store's business people have repeatedly stated that the gates of Jing'an Temple and Tibet Road are merchant's gates. Why should they be closed together, so that the department store cannot operate? Our association believes that this kind of disposal exceeds the scope of what it should be and deliberately obstructs Chinese merchants' business. We should ask you to immediately instruct the police department to open the department store for the restoration of business. We are specially submitting this letter for your information, and we ask you to investigate and deal with it accordingly."

Letter from the Taxpayers' Association 146

The Chinese Taxpayers Association of the Public Concession sent a letter to the General Manager of the工部局(The Shanghai Municipal Council) yesterday, which read: "Dear Sirs, according to reports, your bureau sent police to close the gates of the China National Products United Department Store and prevent business operations. Our association hereby asks your bureau if this kind of emergency disposition has been approved by the主管(supervising) court and according to what legal procedures. We are responding to send a letter to you for your investigation and request that you immediately restore the department store to its original state in order to maintain its business operations and that you clearly answer the above questions."

Citizens' Meeting 147

The First Branch of the Citizens' United Association convened an emergency committee meeting at 10 a.m. yesterday, chaired by Zhou Juchen, and resolved: (1) Send a letter to the工部局(The Shanghai Municipal Council) to reply quickly as to why the National Products Department Store was closed. (2) After receiving a reply, convene a citizens' meeting to solicit opinions. (3) Hold a dinner party on the 17th to discuss the measures first. The letter to the工部局(The Shanghai Municipal Council) is recorded below: "According to a letter from our member, the National Products United Department Store, stating that after our department store took over the New World at the east entrance of Jing'an Temple Road on May 1 and reorganized it into the National Products Department Store, unexpectedly, the工部局(The Shanghai Municipal Council) suddenly sent armed Chinese and foreign detectives from the police station at 3 p.m. on the 9th of this month, without going through legal procedures, to seal all the doors of our department store, prohibit entry and exit, and detain employees, causing them to suffer innocently. We hereby request our association to uphold justice. According to this, our association does not know the truth. After all, how is it? We think your bureau is in charge of public security, and you should not rashly take actions to destroy citizens. We hope that you will give us a quick reply and clearly inform us of the reasons for the封(sealing). This is our earnest prayer." To the English Concession工部局(The Shanghai Municipal Council).

Support from the Labor Community 148

The cigarette industry union, the publishing industry union, the cotton textile industry union, the postal workers' union, and the seafarers' union have initiated the organization of a support association for the National Products Department Store, which was formally established yesterday. An office has been set up, and a discussion meeting will be held at 12 noon today, convening representatives from more than 200 labor unions in the city to discuss everything and prepare to issue an important declaration and a letter to compatriots. In addition, the Chinese medicine industry and other trade associations also replied to the department store yesterday, expressing their willingness to be a backing. Assistance from the Academic Community 149

The student self-governing associations of Jingye Middle School and more than 20 other schools believe that the forced closure of the National Products Department Store is very important. (3) Depart immediately to Pudong, Hunan, Zhabei, and the four rural areas to spread the word and make the public understand the truth.

National Tariff Commission Hires Staff to Study Tariffs 159

The National Tariff Commission believes that the establishment of tariffs is closely related to the prosperity and decline of various industries, but the advantages and disadvantages of which cannot be known to outsiders. In the past, when the government revised tariffs, merchants and the people could not participate in the opinions, and there were always malpractices in the implementation, which was not a way to protect commerce. The commission, in view of the past's faults, now plans to select personnel who are familiar with the business of various industries and tariffs, and give them salaries to study and安(settle). The vice chairman of the commission, Sheng Jun, went to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday for this matter to ask for an introduction. It is heard that the Municipal Chamber of Commerce has transferred letters to the lacquer, fur, cigarette, Western seafood, native cloth, summer cloth, wood, and silk trade associations, asking them to find suitable talents on their behalf. (Xin Sheng She)

County Relocation Design Meeting 165

The Seventh Meeting

The Shanghai County Relocation Design Committee held its seventh meeting at 10:00 a.m. yesterday at the government auditorium. Wu Wenhua presided over the meeting, and Li Tongrui served as the recorder. The proceedings of the meeting are recorded below: A. Reporting Matters: (1) The drawings of the new government buildings have been submitted by the Dafang Construction Company, and the previous instructions have been largely revised. (2) The progress of the construction road plan in the new government area. (3) The Construction Bureau has prepared the budget and circuit diagram for the Puxi telephone plan and submitted it to the County Government for submission to the Construction Department for review. B. Matters for Discussion: (1) The road system in the new government area has been drafted by the Construction Bureau and is divided into five grades according to the road width announced by the Construction Department: A. 16 meters, B. 12 meters, C. 9 meters, D. 6 meters, E. 4 meters. Proposed for discussion. Resolution: Passed. (2) The drawings of the new government buildings do not specify the construction of a one-story staff dormitory. How should it be prepared for construction? Resolution: The Finance Office should jointly convene local people with the Education Bureau to plan and implement it. (3) The drawings of the new government buildings have been completed. How should the bidding process be handled? Resolution: The Construction Bureau should actively proceed under the direction of the County Government. (4) The old streets in Beiqiao should be reorganized with the principle of gradual widening. The Construction Bureau has drafted the Interim Regulations for Reorganizing the New Government Area and the Streets and Rivers of Beiqiao Town, and the Interim Regulations for Suppressing Construction. How should it be decided? (5) Committee Member Wu Wenhua's proposal on incentive measures for various undertakings in the new government area. Resolution: The above two proposals should be discussed together. It was decided that each committee member should sign and note their opinions separately and submit them for discussion at the next meeting. (6) The electricity in the new government area was originally planned to be run by the County Government, but it was deleted due to budget cuts. Now that the telephone and road plans have been largely decided, the electricity project is still missing. How should it be handled? Resolution: The County Government should first contact the China Electric Company and Zhenshi Power Plant separately for further discussion.

Still No Definite News After British Warship Was Hit 168

Haichang Company Inquires Again by Telegram

Whether It Was the Yu Da Is Still Difficult to Confirm

After the Haichang Shipping Bureau's Yu Da ship collided with the British submarine Poseidon, the Haichang Company inquired about the truth again yesterday by telegram. The governments of various countries also telegraphed condolences to the drowned soldiers. The information obtained yesterday is recorded as follows:

Inquiring Again by Telegram: The Haichang Shipping Company, the Shanghai agent of the Yu Da ship, learned from the China Merchants Bureau's Tu Nan ship's radio that the Yu Da ship had collided with a British submarine and telegraphed to inquire. The reply received the day before yesterday did not explain the circumstances of the accident, so it was suspected and could not be decided. At 10:00 p.m. on the 11th, it telegraphed Yingkou to inquire about the truth, saying, "Three hundred items of goods have been opened. It is reported that Da Tu collided and sank a British submarine. Is it true? Reply." By yesterday morning, no reply had been received. At 12:00 a.m., it telegraphed again, saying, "All newspapers are reporting that Da collided and sank a British submarine en route. Is it true? Reply urgently." As of 9:00 p.m., no reply had been received.

Telegraphic Condolences from Various Countries: After the British submarine Poseidon collided and sank with the Yu Da ship 40 miles northwest of Shandong, 18 soldiers drowned. The American submarine Pigeon, under the order of Admiral Markwell, Commander of the U.S. Far East Fleet, rushed to inspect the scene of the accident and arrived yesterday. The governments of the United States, France, Sweden, Spain, Greece, and other countries telegraphed condolences to the drowned soldiers.

Still Difficult to Confirm: A reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency met with Mr. Zhang of the Haichang Company, the agent of the Yu Da ship, yesterday and said that the owner of the Yu Da ship is the Japanese family Jiashi. There are more than 40 people on the ship, including the comprador, chief mate, old track, fireman, sailor, carpenter, and steel worker. Now, the company is inquiring from all parties and has not yet received any news. This time, it does not seem to be the Yu Da ship, or it may be that the Yu Da ship passed through the area and saw another ship colliding and sent a telegram for help on its behalf.

Silk Fabrics Must Be Certified Before Export 172

The Electrical Industry Association Requests Implementation

The Shanghai Electrical Machinery and Silk Weaving Industry Association believes that the export of electrical machinery and silk fabrics is of great importance to international credibility. Yesterday, it specially submitted a request to the Executive Yuan's Ministry of Finance, stating: "In order to maintain national products and emphasize international credibility, we request that silk fabric tax exports be certified by the association. We earnestly request your review and approval. Silk fabrics are our country's major products, and the people's livelihood depends on them. Since the development of the machinery industry, the electrical weaving factories in Shanghai have made great progress, setting a precedent for the country. The association was established several years ago, and it was reorganized in May of last year in accordance with the regulations. Each factory has joined the association in accordance with the regulations. In order to promote the national silk satin, the association urges the industry to improve the quality of manufacturing at any time, especially paying attention to the goods exported overseas. It is not easy to compete in the overseas market. Without excellent goods, how can we win international credibility? Since the National Government promulgated the regulations on tax exemption for silk fabrics, the government's intention to promote prosperity is even more evident. All merchants are ecstatic and will have further struggles in the overseas market. However, the Shanghai area is vast, and it is inevitable that there will be profiteers who reduce labor and steal materials in order to seek personal gain. As a result, the products are shoddy and the sizes are insufficient. Not only do they fail to live up to the government's encouragement, but the entire international credibility will be harmed. If we do not find a way to plan early, the harm will be unimaginable. The association has the responsibility to supervise and guide factories. Since we have something to see, we dare not be silent to the superiors. We propose that after the implementation of the tax exemption regulations, all electrical silk fabrics produced in Shanghai should first obtain certification from the association from the customs before being allowed to export tax-free, so as to avoid shoddy goods, loss of international credibility, and to maintain national products and prevent loopholes. It is for public convenience."

Grain Stores Should Be Exempt From Business Tax 174

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Sent a Letter to the Municipal Finance Bureau's Business Tax Preparation Office Yesterday, Stating: "Dear Sir, On the 11th of this month, we received a letter from the Municipal Rice Store Association, stating that our industry is a grain store merchant, and we have paid tooth tax and received a license to open a store. According to Article 20 of the draft regulations on business tax collection in the city, all existing donations and taxes in the city that are similar in nature to business shall be renamed business tax and shall be temporarily collected at the old tax rate. Furthermore, on the 7th of this month, it was reported that the Legislative Yuan passed the Business Tax Law, and Article 10 stipulates that the tooth tax, pawn tax, slaughter tax, and other business taxes that should be banned or strictly prohibited in accordance with the law in various provinces and cities may be temporarily changed to business tax at the original tax rate. Then, after the business tax is levied in the city, our industry's former tooth tax and license tax will undoubtedly be changed to business tax at the original tax rate. However, the tax rate passed by the city also lists a grain industry item, which collects 1/1000 of the business turnover. This seems to be redundant to the previous regulations. I don't know whether the 1/1000 tax rate for the grain industry belongs to the scope of grain store merchants who changed from the original tooth tax to business tax. We earnestly request that your office transfer to the Association for a detailed explanation as soon as possible so that there is something to follow." The association received the letter. According to Article 11 of the supplementary measures to the outline of the Ministry's determination of the collection of business tax in various provinces, the first step is to change the tax of tooth, pawn, slaughter, etc. to business tax and collect it at the original tax rate. It is stipulated that those who have paid the tooth tax and license tax will no longer be taxed separately for business tax. This is the regulation stipulated by the Ministry. Since Doumi Bank has already received a license to open a store and paid the tooth tax, it is a natural interpretation that it does not need to pay business tax anymore. The newly promulgated business tax regulations in this city have a grain industry listed in the sales business. The Doumi Bank, which has paid the tooth tax and license tax, should not be included in it. The association requests an explanation to dispel doubts and should send a letter to your office to investigate and show a reply, so as to transfer it. This is the most fortunate."

The Chinese Taxpayers' Association, for the Public Works Department's collection of police donations, should notify the taxpayers in advance more than 14 days in advance. Yesterday, it sent another letter to the Public Works Department, saying, "Dear Sir, Before the collection of all municipal general donations, we believe that the principle of equal treatment has been followed, and all taxpayers have been notified in writing, allowing a 14-day grace period. However, the association has repeatedly received reports from taxpayers, saying that they have not received the above-mentioned written notice, and personnel from your bureau have gone to collect donations, etc. In the association's opinion, your bureau has repeatedly declared that there is no discriminatory treatment among taxpayers, then the 14-day advance notice must have been handled uniformly, otherwise, would it not be a real evidence of discriminatory treatment? Therefore, the association firmly believes that your bureau is not insincere, and the above-mentioned report may be due to the negligence of the delivery person of your bureau. We should send a letter, hoping to check and give us a true reply." Sincerely, Shanghai Public Concession Public Works Department.

The Tax Rules Meeting Requested Exemption From the Seal Bamboo Shoot Tooth Tax 177

The Tax Rules Research Committee of the Municipal Industry Association sent a letter to the Finance Bureau yesterday requesting approval to exempt the seal bamboo shoot industry from the tooth tax, saying, "Dear Sir, According to the letter from the seal bamboo shoot industry association, the tooth tax has been followed from the old view of the late Qing Dynasty. The origin of its tax rules is actually similar to the business tax rules. At this time of reform of public administration, all harsh and miscellaneous donations are being exempted everywhere. If each industry's business must be licensed, that is the evidence of business. If we collect tooth tax again, it is inevitable that it is repeated. Moreover, such as our seal bamboo shoot industry, in recent years, most of them are self-releasing Zhuangke to purchase from Fujian, which is actually a kind of transportation of local goods and is not a temporary commission. We should be exempted from the item of tooth tax, etc. "According to this, we found that the industry's business is purely for transportation and is very different from the intermediary merchants who set up lines to collect commissions. There is no need to pay for a job. Moreover, the newly promulgated business tax rate in the city also has an item of seal bamboo shoot industry tax of 1/1000. It is also necessary to remove the tooth tax to avoid one industry and two taxes. The letter from the previous letter should be given to your bureau to approve the exemption of the industry's tooth tax, so as to avoid double taxation and maintain commerce. This is the most grateful." Sincerely, Shanghai Municipal Finance Bureau.

Foreign Merchants Request to Maintain the Trademark Office 179

The Shanghai Office of the Trademark Bureau of the Ministry of Industry notified various agencies and businesses on the 2nd that the Shanghai Office would be abolished at the end of this month and merged with the Nanjing Trademark Bureau. The general business felt inconvenient. The Ministry of Industry has been petitioning to continue to maintain the Shanghai Bureau in order to facilitate commercial difficulties. Recently, foreign lawyer He Lemang, because he represents foreign merchants in handling many trademark cases, specially wrote to Director Wen of the Shanghai Office, saying, "Dear Sir, We have recently received your bureau's notification of June this year, saying that the Shanghai Branch of the Trademark Bureau will be abolished at the end of this month, and that the branch will stop working after the 15th, etc. After receiving the notification, this office is very worried, because the Shanghai Branch is very convenient for the general merchants, and it serves a large number of merchants related to trademarks. Once it is abolished, it will be very inconvenient. I think the director knows that Shanghai is the commercial center of the country. In fact, almost no trademark is used in China that is not related to Shanghai. Now, your bureau's general agency is located in the capital, which is justified, but the Shanghai branch provides many conveniences for the general people's trademark registration, and it is urgent to abolish this agency. It is really confusing. The Birch Office handles many trademark cases, and the various merchants also unanimously request your bureau to approve the continued maintenance of the Shanghai branch. I hope that you will carefully review our office's request as being justified and for public convenience."

Expansion of the Guanghua Dyeing Factory Strike 181

Seventeen Workers, Including Yan A'er, Arrested

Municipal Social Affairs Bureau to Convene Mediation Today

The Guanghua Machinery Dyeing Factory on Luban Road in this city, due to the reinstatement of worker Zhu Linhou, has stirred up the anger of the workers, resulting in the assault of factory manager Gu Yongquan. The factory was forced to announce a temporary shutdown. Since the day before yesterday, all 300-plus workers have been living inside the factory, guarding the factory gate. Health Bureau Notifies Physicians of Procedures for Outpatient Visits to the French Concession 182

The Shanghai Physicians' Association and the Chinese Medical Association received a letter yesterday from the Municipal Health Bureau stating: "Regarding the French Concession's implementation of physician registration, many of the established regulations are improper. This Bureau has repeatedly made serious representations and has obtained the following substantial results: (1) Only one license fee of two yuan is required. (2) Physicians who do not reside or have clinics within the concession and hold formal documents from this Bureau may make outpatient visits within the French Concession without having to register or obtain a license from the French Concession." When this Bureau negotiated with the French Concession, it proposed supplementary measures to prevent unqualified doctors from passing themselves off as qualified, namely, that all physicians should photograph their certificates and this Bureau's business registration license in six-inch film to be carried with them when making outpatient visits to the French Concession for inspection by French Concession inspectors at any time. However, this Bureau is deeply concerned that such films could easily be faked and is instead using a small, easy-to-carry license. All physicians who already have a physician's certificate and this Bureau's business registration license can bring a two-inch, half-body photograph of themselves to this Bureau to obtain a small photo, completely free of charge, except for the one-cent stamp duty that must be paid. Physicians who have not obtained a business registration license may obtain a small photo when obtaining a business registration license. This Bureau is currently rushing to produce these small photos, and a letter will be sent to inform you when they are ready for collection. This letter is sent first for your information."

Jisheng Society Relief Grain Arrives in Mianchi 185

To Be Distributed in Zones Immediately

The Chinese Jisheng Society, considering the severity of the disaster in Mianchi, Henan, allocated 55,000 yuan for relief. The number of people is too large to provide relief to everyone, so it has been changed to distributing relief grain, which can save more people, as reported previously. Now, a report has been received from Feng Yangshan, director of relief in the county, stating that millet was purchased in Zhengzhou for 30 catties per yuan, green beans for 28 catties per yuan, mung beans for 28 catties per yuan, and wheat for 29 catties per yuan, which is about half the price in Mianchi. 190 tons have been purchased, worth about 14,000 yuan, transported by cart to Mianchi, and have now arrived in Mianchi. They will be immediately transported to the three disaster areas in the east, south, and west for distribution. Once this distribution is complete, the most severely affected areas in the north will be investigated for effective relief. With the grain price being much cheaper than in Mianchi, the number of people saved can be doubled. With this, the disaster victims can temporarily alleviate their current living conditions. Director Feng's previous letter stated that the society has withdrawn 22,000 yuan from the Bank of China in Zhengzhou, which the society has now remitted to the Bank of China in this city.

Jianghua and Yamato Collision Case 187

Negotiations Unlikely to Escalate

The China Merchants Bureau's Yangtze River ship Jianghua, after leaving the dock for repairs at the Jiangnan Shipyard on the 28th of last month, sailed to Pucheng in Xinkai River and encountered the Dada Company's Yamato entering the port and anchoring to turn around. Due to the rapid rising tide, the two ships collided, as reported previously. It is now learned that both parties have submitted reports from their captains as a basis for negotiation, but each party holds a different opinion, and no results have been achieved. Distributing Reactionary Leaflets 191

The Offenders Sentenced Separately

The Communist Party members Tang Shaoji, Zhou Li'an, Gu Hanliang, Yang Shichang, Lu Jinshui, etc., on the evening of the other day, under the guise of watching a movie in a certain cinema in the French Concession, distributed reactionary leaflets and set off firecrackers. The theater staff discovered this and reported it to the police, who ordered detectives to go to the scene, arrest Tang and others, and confiscate the leaflets. Communist Party books were also confiscated from Tang's residence and brought to the police station. Suspects Zhou Zhilian, Zhou Rongchu, Wang Weicheng, etc., were subsequently arrested. Yesterday, they were sent to the French Court for investigation. The police chief first went to the court, explained the situation, and presented the confiscated leaflets and books. Subsequently, Fan Quangen and other tea boys from the theater went to the court to testify about the defendants' distribution of leaflets. When questioned, Tang Shaoji confessed that Zhao, who is at large, had indeed instigated the people to distribute reactionary leaflets in the cinema. Zhou Li'an, Gu Hanliang, and Yang Shichang also confessed. The people stated that although they went to the cinema to watch a movie, they did not know about the distribution of leaflets. The judge asked, "If you did not distribute leaflets, why were Communist books found in your residence?" Zhou and the others were speechless. Lu Jinshui stated that the people went to the cinema with Yang Shichang on that day and knew that they were distributing leaflets, but the people did not participate and asked for leniency. Zhou Zhilian, Zhou Rongchu, and Wang Weicheng all stated that although the people knew Tang and the others, they did not know about the distribution of leaflets. The Chinese and Western judges sentenced Tang Shaoji to two years in the Western Prison, Zhou Li'an, Gu Hanliang, and Yang Shichang to one year each, and Lu to six months. Upon completion of their terms, all will be permanently expelled from the concession. Zhou Zhilian and the other three were permanently deported. The confiscated leaflets and books were all confiscated.

Local News Two

The Son of Paint Merchant Wang Zhengguo, Wang Ruibao, Was Kidnapped Yesterday 197

Involving the Chinese, British, and French Concessions

Student Kidnapped by Fake Automobile

Yesterday morning around six o'clock, a case of bandits hijacking a car and kidnapping a primary school student suddenly occurred. The location of the incident is related to the Chinese, British, and French concessions. The bandits rented a car on Zhapu Road in the Public Concession, the hostage lived on Zhonghua Road in the Chinese area, and the kidnapping took place near Xinqiao Street in the French Concession. The detailed process is recorded as follows:

Wang Ruibao's School Time, Wang Zhengguo, a wealthy paint merchant from Ningbo, nearly fifty years old, resides at 1451 Zhonghua Road in the Chinese area. He has a son named Ruibao, who is sixteen years old and is a fourth-grade student in the primary school department of the Qianye Middle School on Tiemalu, Penglu Road in the Public Concession. He must go to school at seven o'clock every morning, rain or shine.

Male and Female Hired a Car Yesterday morning at six o'clock, a well-dressed man and woman, seemingly a couple, suddenly came to Zhongshan Automobile Co., Ltd. at 295 Zhapu Road. The woman was holding a baby in her arms and said that they needed to hire a car to send them to Xietu Road in the Chinese area near Avenue Albert in the French Concession. The company's cashier ordered the car driver Wang Youfu to drive a No. 12604 city number 864 covered car to the address.

Xietu Road Payment Situation The car driver Wang Youfu drove the car to Avenue Albert, then straight south through Xujiahui Road, over the bridge from Meixie Road, and straight to Xietu Road. At a remote place, the passengers ordered the car to stop. Then, they took out two silver dollars from their pockets and ordered the car driver to give change. The driver replied that he did not carry change. The passengers nodded and told the driver to get out of the car and follow them to get the money. The driver obeyed and got out of the car.

Car Driver's Detention Time After the driver got out of the car, two burly men suddenly jumped out from the roadside, each showing a pistol, and flanked him from the left and right, prohibiting him from making a sound. Threatened by their power, the driver had no way to resist, so he followed the two men into the nearby wilderness, while the car renters themselves acted as drivers, turned the car around, and sped away as if flying, disappearing in an instant. Later, the driver was detained for about an hour before being released.

Stop the Car and Wait for the Hostage After being released, the car driver immediately ran to report to the Public Security Bureau. At this time, the bandits had already obtained the car and were waiting near the Siming Guild Hall in the French Concession, waiting for the hostage to come.

The Little Hostage is Still Missing Yesterday morning at six-thirty, Wang Zhengguo's son, Ruibao, took his own chartered car to school. Unexpectedly, when he arrived near the Siming Guild Hall on Xinqiao Street in the French Concession, four bandits suddenly came, showed pistols, grabbed Ruibao from the chartered car, and dragged him to a car parked on the side of the road, which flew away. Seeing his young master being kidnapped, the driver of the chartered car couldn't help but panic and ran back to report to the owner, who went to the Public Security Bureau and the police station to request an interception, but there has been no news of it as of this morning.

True Picture of the Yi People in Sichuan Border Area 198

Special Reporter of This Newspaper Photographed

The Sichuan border areas have long been inhabited by Yi tribes. Only a small part of them were assimilated after the conquest of the Greater and Lesser Jinchuan during the Qianlong period of the Qing Dynasty, while the rest remained wilderness. Last year, this newspaper specially sent Wang Xiaoting and Liu Shuofu to the Sichuan border area to collect the true picture of the lives of the Yi people in various places. From November of last winter to now, it has been more than six months. They have traveled long distances and ventured deep into the various Yi tribes in western Sichuan, northern Sichuan, southern Sichuan, Qiang Yi, Tibetan Yi, and the most ferocious Luo Yi, taking various films, such as Yi people's houses, Yi people's clothing, Yi people's lives, and the strange and dangerous mountains and gorges, hundreds of miles of high mountains and rivers. Because of the investigation of the Kang Tibetan war, they ventured to the front line of Daofu in western Sichuan to take films about the truth of the war and the situations that are not understood outside. There is also the second highest mountain in the world, the Mount Gongga with an altitude of more than 25,000 feet. Mr. Wang is the first Chinese person to photograph it. Recently, a letter from the two gentlemen stated that in recent years, the Luo Yi in southern Sichuan have often kidnapped people and seized land. The area near Mabian is occupied by the Luo Yi. Military affairs have been frequent. Dozens of miles were recovered starting this spring. Hearing that the Luo Yi are seeking peace, they went to Mabian again, all the way to the border of the recovered land, and after many dangers, they finally took many films that have never been seen outside. The Luo Yi live in caves and are extremely fierce and savage among the Yi tribes. In the past, many foreigners who entered the country were killed by them. In the travelogues of Westerners, they are regarded as an extremely barbaric nation. In addition to recording and photographing, the two gentlemen also carried a motion picture camera to take films. A telegram has been received recently stating that they will return to Shanghai next week. In the future, the publication will definitely make an extremely valuable contribution to the customs of the Sichuan border area.

Discovery of Soldiers Shot by Bandits in Weiting 199

Patrol Route Encounters Bandits

Li Guocai and Shen Lisheng Died

On the 1st of this month, near the Weiting Railway Station, bandits opened fire and wounded two road protection soldiers. On that day, the road protection soldiers Li Guocai and Shen Lisheng were patrolling along the railway and found two people, A and B, who looked like bandits. As they were about to step forward to search them, the bandits fired several shots first, wounding Li and Shen and causing them to fall to the ground before fleeing. The station sent the two wounded soldiers to Shanghai and transferred them to the Tongren Hospital for treatment. One soldier, Li Guocai, died on the afternoon of the 7th due to injuries to vital organs. The body was transported by car to the autopsy office. The Special District Court was reported and sent a prosecutor to verify the body and place it in a coffin. Another soldier, Shen Lisheng from Changzhou, was sent to the hospital. Although the doctor took out the bullet (with the letters C and the number 600 engraved on it), the injury was internal. The treatment was ineffective, and he died of his injuries yesterday. The hospital has notified the police station to send the body to the autopsy office for verification. At the same time, the garrison headquarters has issued an order for a thorough investigation.

Qian Baosheng Commits Suicide with Camphor Balls 200

Frustrated and Unable to Achieve His Goals

Fortunately, He Was Rescued and Saved His Life

Qian Baosheng, a native of Luodian, was nineteen years old. He used to work in Ziyangguan in Shanghai, but recently he quit his job. The day before yesterday, he heard that his father was at a relative's house in Songjiang, so he went to Songjiang at 10:00 p.m. Upon learning that his father had already returned home, he checked into room No. 5 of the Xin Travel Agency on Nanchang Road, paid the room fee, and went out. Before long, he returned to the room and went to sleep. Unexpectedly, he had secretly taken several camphor balls, intending to commit suicide. At around 2:00 a.m., he groaned due to poisoning. The waiter, because the neighboring guest was not asleep, passed by room No. 5 and became suspicious. He immediately reported it to the innkeeper, who went into the room to inquire and saw that Qian's complexion was different and his words were vague. He was sent to the Seashore Public Hospital. After the doctor's diagnosis, he learned that he had swallowed camphor balls. Yesterday, he was cured by the hospital. The innkeeper sent someone to Luodian to inform his father and sent his brother to Songjiang to take him home. When asked about the reason for his suicide, it was said that although Baosheng was young, he had very high aspirations. He had recently lost his job, causing all his hopes to vanish, so he was angry and resorted to this extreme measure.

Poor Jiang Fukang 201

Economic Hardship After Unemployment

Rescued After Throwing Himself into the Wusong River

Wrote a Very Painful Letter to His Parents

Said He Wanted to Become a Dog or Horse in the Next Life

At around 10:50 p.m. the night before last, a person suddenly jumped into the river from the Yunzaobang Bridge in Wusong, intending to commit suicide. He happened to be spotted by guard Liu Lunxuan, who immediately called nearby fishing boats to rescue him. Fortunately, he had not drunk too much water. After being resuscitated, he gradually woke up and was taken to the First Station of the Seventh District of the Public Security Bureau. Yesterday morning, after questioning by Director Zhang, he stated that his name was Jiang Fukang, he was thirty-two years old, and he was from Sanbei, Ningbo. He had left his hometown for four or five years and had been making a living outside, only able to support himself. Recently, he had been suffering from illness and unemployment, and his economic situation was becoming increasingly dire. He was ragged and had no face to return to his hometown to see his parents, wife, and children. Yesterday, he took a bus to Songjiang and could not find his friend. For a time, he had no way to go, so he had the idea of ending his life. Now, he was fortunate to be rescued and requested to be settled, etc. A suicide note was found next to him, written to the Jiang Tongshun Pawnshop on Nannanmen Street, Guanhaiwei, Cibei, Ningbo. The letter was addressed to his parents. There were many typos in the letter, indicating that he only knew a little about writing and barely managed to write his general meaning, saying that he had been away from his parents for five years. He wanted to make something of himself outside but could not. You two are old. Buy some food if you want to eat. Make some clothes if you want to wear. I will not make something of myself in this life. I will definitely be reborn as a dog or a horse in the next life to repay you two. I am sick outside now, and my clothes and food are exhausted. I have no choice but to throw myself into the river to commit suicide. Parents, do not be sad, etc. Director Zhang immediately ordered the police to send a report to the General Bureau for disposition.

American Radio Industry Giant Arrives in Shanghai 202

Mr. Nall, President of the American United Radio Corporation

Mr. Nall, President of the American United Radio Corporation, traveled the world with his wife this spring, departing from New York to inspect the branches of the company in various countries and to visit the scenery of various places. He arrived in Shanghai on the 5th of this month, transferring from Beijing and Nanjing, and stayed at the Cathay Hotel in the Sassoon Building. He took the opportunity to visit the Zhenru International Radio Station of the Ministry of Communications and the Lao Beimen Shanghai Radio Station, and was quite satisfied. He will now go to Xiaoluzong and other places for inspection and left Shanghai on the Canadian Empress the day before yesterday. He will return to Shanghai in early next month and then return to the United States. Mr. Nall is now seventy-two years old, but he is energetic and vigorous, like a young man. On the left is a photograph of Mr. and Mrs. Nall and Mrs. Zhu Qiqing when they boarded the ship at the New Customs Wharf. Mr. Nall's experience is recorded as follows:

Mr. Nall was born in Fredericksburg, USA, in 1859. He was gifted and at the age of sixteen, he was only a messenger boy for the Western Union Telegraph Company. Due to his hard work, he was transferred to St. Louis and assigned as the director of the local Edison Telephone Branch. During his tenure, he proposed building a telegraph trunk line along the transcontinental railroad. After his detailed plan, it was finally completed step by step from 1880 to 1900. The number of telegraph offices across the country suddenly increased by thousands, and tens of thousands of people depended on it for a living. It was all the work of one person. At that time, the operator of this project was the Postal Telegraph-Cable Company, and he served as the manager and vice president of the company for a total of twenty-five years. Later, when radio was invented, he saw its importance and first initiated the organization of a commercial radio company in New York in 1913. It was finally established in 1914, named the American Marconi Wireless Telegraph Company. He resigned from his position at the Postal Telegraph-Cable Company and was appointed as the manager and vice president of the new company. All operations were very ingenious. That year, he established direct radio communication between Japan and the United States, opening the era of international commercial radio telegraph. Radio became increasingly prominent. After that, through his plan, direct radio communications were established between the United States and the United Kingdom, Norway, Germany, and France, which was of great importance to the future of American telecommunications. The development of American commercial radio today is due to the contribution of Mr. Nall. In 1919, the American radio industry formed the American United Radio Corporation in New York, and he was elected as the president and CEO of the company. At the same time, he served as the president or CEO of the Radio Publishing House and other companies. In 1922, the Elsea International Radio Society was established. In 1923, the Commercial International Radio Association was established. He was elected as the general director of the association, etc. Due to his advanced age, he retired in 1928, but he is still a director of the American United Radio Corporation, etc.

Gui Lansun Sues Huang's Two Sons

Request for Recovery of House Construction Costs

Yesterday, Gui Lansun, acting as a contractor, retained lawyer Lu Shaozong as his representative and stated in a lawsuit to the French Court that the late Huang Chujiu had entered into a contract with the plaintiff to build a house at the corner of Rue Sainte-Marie and Route Tenant de la Tour, with a total construction cost of 29,000 taels, specifying that 5,000 taels would be paid each time, with the first payment due after the foundation was laid. Subsequently, the plaintiff proceeded according to the contract. Upon completion of the first stage of construction, the plaintiff requested payment of the construction cost, but it was delayed, and Huang subsequently passed away. Therefore, the plaintiff filed a lawsuit requesting that Huang Zixianyao and Huang Xianzhong, Huang's two sons, be ordered to recover the full amount in accordance with the contract, as well as all losses and interest. The defendants, Huang Xianyao and Huang Xianzhong, represented by lawyer Tan Yigong, admitted the existence of this debt, but stated that all of Huang's assets had been transferred to accountants Pan Zhaobang and Wu Zheng for liquidation, and requested the court to merge this case into Huang's liquidation proceedings.

Judge Gong ordered a postponement for further review.

Ten Years of Cohabitation Turn Sour 212

It Seems Difficult to Renew Old Ties

Chen Xiufeng, the sister of a comprador Chen on the Japanese steamer Daifuku Maru, nearly thirty-nine years old, went to the Puwo Village in Zhujia Muqiao, Zhabei, and because she went to the tobacco and paper shop at the entrance of the alley every day, she became inexplicably involved with Feng Ming, a relative of the shop owner. Later, when her brother heard about it, he severely scolded her. Xiufeng took the opportunity to take her belongings and eloped with Feng, renting a house together as if they were husband and wife. This has been going on for ten years. At first, they were very harmonious. However, since last spring, they suddenly began to suspect each other. Chen accused Feng of having a new love, and Feng accused Chen of adultery with a man named Chen Arong. As a result, they went from quarreling to litigation. Feng sued Chen for restricting freedom, and after the court's investigation, Chen was declared not guilty. Chen sued Feng for seduction, abandonment, false accusation, and added a civil suit to recover 9,000 yuan in alimony and 3,000 yuan in damages for reputation loss. The case was heard in court yesterday afternoon by Judge Cheng of the Special District Local Court. Because the two parties were not formally married, but had been living together for ten years, the judge advised them to resolve the matter peacefully, considering their past relationship. Feng immediately expressed his willingness to give the plaintiff 300 yuan to end the relationship. However, Chen hoped for 1,000 yuan, and the amount was too different, so they could not reach a settlement. The lawyers for both parties then began their arguments and concluded. Judge Cheng then declared the defendant not guilty. The civil part of the case will be transferred to the civil court for hearing.

Iron Factory Foreman Steals Car Model, Exposure 214

The China Iron Factory, located west of the Wusong Yunzaobang, has recently seen thriving business due to the high price of silver and demand from silk weaving factories in various ports for custom-made silk twisting machines, thread winding machines, and towel machines. Silk weaving factories are happy to purchase these machines because they are comparable to imported goods but are much cheaper. It is said that the factory foreman, Jiang Ruisheng, who has been employed at the factory for four or five years, saw that these machines had a wide market and high profits, and intended to manufacture them outside the factory to get rich. Therefore, while working at the factory, he stole three iron models and two wooden models of the machine, wrapped them in his clothes, and had a worker named Su Tiansheng take them to Shanghai the other evening. When they arrived at Yunzaobang Bridge, they were discovered by a police officer on duty and taken back to the No. 1 Section of the Seventh District of the Public Security Bureau. Under questioning, Su confessed that the foreman Jiang Ruisheng had asked him to send them to Shanghai. The section then notified the China Iron Factory to detain the foreman and send him to the section for detention. Currently, because General Manager Lu Chengshu is not in Shanghai, they must wait for Manager Lu to return to Shanghai to investigate who instigated the theft of the registered trademark, intending to counterfeit and disrupt business. The factory will file a lawsuit in court to warn against imitation.

Sending a Child is Actually Child Trafficking 216

Xinghua People Kidnap Pootung People

Zhang Jiangzhen is Five Years Old

Chen Wu, a Fujianese woman, nineteen years old, residing at No. 4 Sheng'an Lane, Meizhu Street, South City, was visited the other day by an acquaintance from Xinghua County named Wu Yuzhen, who was holding a lively and lovely girl, about four or five years old, wearing luxurious clothes and leather shoes. Wu said that the child needed to be temporarily left in her care, and that after a few days, she would be taken back to her hometown. Because they were both acquainted, Wu did not ask about the child's background and agreed to take her in. Unexpectedly, after Wu Yuzhen left, the child cried all day long and refused to eat. Fearing that there was something hidden and that complications might arise later, Wu notified the watchman He Yushi of the 11th post that evening around midnight and took the child to the 3rd Section of the 1st District. Chief Jin questioned her about the situation. He immediately dispatched police to bring Wu Yuzhen in for preliminary interrogation. Wu confessed that she was forty years old, residing at Zhengjia Muqiao in the Public Concession, and worked as a cook. Last month, an acquaintance named Wang Ar Er came and said that he had a granddaughter (referring to the girl) named Xiuying, who was five years old. Because her parents were both dead, and his family was poor and struggling, he was unable to raise her and was planning to sell her. At that time, because Wu lacked children, she agreed. Wang Li, Chen Zhou, and Cai Chang, an old woman who ran a matchmaking shop at No. 84 Langjia Bridge outside Datongmen, acted as intermediaries. She paid 60 yuan to buy the girl and temporarily left her at Chen Wu's house. The girl said that her name was Zhang Jiangzhen, five years old, from Pootung, and that she had a mommy and daddy at home. It was observed that the child did not look like she came from a poor family, and her statements were completely different from Wu's confession, clearly indicating that there was something false and incomplete in the situation. Because the matter concerned the sale of people, it was ordered that they be detained pending further investigation.

Letter 223

Dear Editor, I have read in your newspaper on June 6 that the Municipal Health Bureau, in order to prevent harm from mad dogs, has formulated regulations for the elimination of stray dogs. Dog owners are asked to apply for licenses, with a license fee of 50 cents per head in the urban area and 25 cents in the rural area. This does not conform to the original text. After checking our Bureau's announcement, it is written that the license fee is one yuan per head in the urban area, and half price, five jiao per head, in the rural area. Please correct this immediately to avoid miscommunication. I hope you will take note. Sincerely, Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau, June 12.
